Students from various schools set out to seal up all Japanese goods that had not been sold within a time limit by various merchants. Japanese goods have been completely eliminated from the market. The attack was repelled after the North Bank Fort fired two cannons. The First Brigade and Second Regiment of the army have opened Ma Jiang, and Liu Heding also telegraphed that the Li Regiment of the 334th Regiment will arrive in the province this morning. Speculation suggests that the silver loan may be brought up again. However, those familiar with the American financial situation said that American banks have not been overstocked in the past three months. Lin's arrival should not be for the silver loan. Xu Yongchang, Fu Zuoyi, and others visited Zhang several times to discuss military and political affairs in North China. Zhang personally visited Xu yesterday and talked for a long time. Qilu University Granted Approval for Registration

(Jinan) The Ministry of Education ordered the Education Department that the private Qilu University in the city be approved for registration. However, it ordered that the Theology Department be separated and that students should not be forced or persuaded to study religious subjects. The school is currently divided into three colleges: Liberal Arts, Science, and Medicine, with an affiliated Republican Hospital. Its Theology Department has been renamed Qilu Theological Seminary. Soviet

Opening of the Central Executive Committee

Over Six Hundred Members in Attendance

Discussing the Guiding Principles for Future Governance

Situation in Eastern Provinces Increasingly Perilous

Molotov Criticizes the League of Nations

National News Agency, Moscow, 22nd – The Central Executive Committee of the Soviet Union, with over six hundred members,

will gather tonight in the resplendent ballroom of the Grand Kremlin Palace for the opening ceremony. The committee's main function is to approve government achievements, possessing limited real power, but its political and moral influence is significant, akin to that of a parliament in other countries. Government officials will report on the political situation, followed by discussions within the committee. The reports are expected to be unanimously approved, but the sentiments expressed by the committee will serve as a guiding principle for governance in the coming months. Tonight, the presidium will consist of seven chairpersons, with Kalinin representing the Russian Federation. The other six federal chairpersons will take turns presiding over the meetings. The Chairman of the Council of People's Commissars, Molotov, whose position is equivalent to that of a prime minister, will be seated alongside other government leaders on the presidium. At the other end will be diplomatic personnel and foreign correspondents attending as observers, numbering twenty-five. Apart from the National Congress of Soviets, this committee is considered the most representative national assembly. Many members will attend in their native attire, displaying a diverse and colorful array of garments. There will be many women. The Central Executive Committee was elected by the National Congress of Soviets in March of this year, divided into two groups: one being the Union Council, comprising four hundred and sixty-nine members, elected according to population; the other being the Council of Nationalities, comprising one hundred and thirty-eight members, representing each republic, regardless of territory or population. The two councils will hold a joint session tonight, and thereafter will convene separately. National News Agency, Moscow, 22nd – The Premier of the Soviet Russian Federation, Molotov, made a statement today at the Central Executive Committee, ridiculing the League of Nations' pretense of seeking a solution to the Manchurian Incident. Molotov's speech was delivered in the presence of diplomatic representatives from various countries stationed in Russia. His words were firm, and the audience erupted in applause, making his remarks particularly significant. Molotov vehemently denied that the international community had taken any action to mitigate the disaster of the Manchurian Incident. Molotov further stated that the organization not only failed to alleviate the disaster but also exacerbated the situation in Manchuria. "We initially had low expectations, but we did not anticipate the effects would be so dire," he said. Molotov expressed pessimism about the upcoming disarmament conference next year, stating that it would be nothing more than a gathering of major powers, aiming not to reduce armaments but to expand them.

National News Agency, Moscow, 22nd – At the annual meeting of the Soviet Union's Central Executive Committee held in the Kremlin Palace tonight, the fear of war in the Far East was also mentioned. Before Chairman Petrovsky delivered the opening remarks and welcomed the representatives, Stalin suddenly appeared on the podium, triggering a thunderous ovation that lasted five minutes. Petrovsky then continued his speech, detailing the achievements of the first three years of the Five-Year Plan and the proposed undertakings for the next two years. He stated that as Soviet Russia embarked on industrial and agricultural progress and recruited millions of new workers for social construction, the middle class was collapsing. "Today, we only see the capitalist nations gradually approaching their demise, with the living standards of their workers declining daily. Therefore, they are desperately competing for world markets. As their interests clash, they are preparing for imperialist wars – a war in the Far East, a war against Russia." At this point, Petrovsky's tone became increasingly severe as he addressed the diplomatic corps, stating, "Soviet Russia is fully prepared to defend against all attacks. The Soviet government and the Soviet Communist Party will lead the people to complete the Five-Year Plan in four years." After Petrovsky's speech, the Executive Committee unanimously approved the agenda, which focused on economic matters and, in particular, plans for the coming year.

Sixtieth Session

Diet Convened Yesterday in Japan

Victory for the Minseitō Party in the Election of the Speaker

Labor Party Demands Dissolution of the Diet

Dentsu News Agency, Tokyo, 23rd – The anticipated dissolution of the Sixtieth Diet was convened today. Due to the Seiyūkai party, being in the minority after the cabinet reshuffle, the opposition Minseitō Party, holding a majority, will engage in a fierce struggle with the government. After the House of Representatives convened at 10:00 AM, Secretary-General Taguchi assumed the speaker's chair, reported on all matters, and commenced the election of the speaker. The Seiyūkai nominated Den Sugawara, while the Minseitō nominated Keijirō Nakamura. As a result of the secret ballot, Nakamura was elected as the first speaker candidate with a majority, and Sugawara was elected with the next highest number of votes. The session adjourned at 11:10 AM. In the afternoon, Yoshiichi Masuda of the Minseitō Party was elected Vice-Speaker.

Japan Federation News Agency, Tokyo, 23rd – The House of Peers convened at 9:00 AM on the same morning, with Speaker Tokugawa retaining his position.

Dentsu News Agency, Tokyo, 23rd – A group of executives from the Japan Labor-Farmer Mass Party, including Hisashi Asō and Juichō Miwa, visited Prime Minister Inukai in the morning at 11:00 AM as representatives of the party. Citing the economic crisis and the Manchurian Incident, they expressed strong opposition to the Sixtieth Diet's imperialist policies, which would increase the burden on the proletariat, and demanded immediate dissolution of the Diet. Reuters, Tokyo, 23rd – An announcement was made today stating that the Diet is scheduled to formally convene on December 26th. However, the business on that day will be purely formal, and the session will adjourn for the year-end holidays on the 27th, reconvening on January 21st. At that time, fierce debates are expected. If the government does not dissolve the Diet, significant events are anticipated. There is much speculation in political circles regarding the dissolution issue, but the general consensus is that the current government will not collapse. Both major parties in the House of Representatives, in light of the domestic and international situation, wish to avoid dissolution of the Diet. There are proposals to form a special body consisting of key figures from both parties to ensure the successful implementation of national policies and avoid the need to appeal to the people.

The Vatican

Renowned Library Collapses

Loss of Books and Artworks Beyond Estimation

Five Librarians Buried in the Rubble

Weak Wall Support Leads to Disaster

National News, Rome, 22nd – Today, a portion of the roof of the Vatican Library in the Holy City suddenly collapsed. It was dusk, and readers had not yet left. Cracks appeared in the upper roof, causing those who saw them to scream and rush for the doors. However, five librarians were unable to escape and were buried beneath over twenty thousand volumes. It is not yet known if any readers were among the victims. The sudden incident was as loud as thunder, and the entire Holy City heard it, expressing shock and grief. The cause of the disaster is attributed to the numerous steel bookshelves recently donated to the library by the United States. Initially, the Pope, upon receiving the donation, was concerned that the aging structure might not be able to bear the weight of the bookshelves. Therefore, he commissioned workers to reinforce it. However, the foundation of that section of the building was not strong enough, leading to this tragedy.

Reuters, Vatican City, 22nd – A large portion of the world-renowned Vatican Library collapsed this afternoon. The fire brigade is currently working valiantly to search for people buried in the rubble. The library houses many precious artworks and some of the world's most valuable manuscripts, making the loss inestimable. At least ten thousand volumes of books are buried in the rubble, about a quarter of the library's collection. It is believed that those buried are students working at the library. Rescue teams are now digging through bricks and tiles to rescue the trapped individuals. The collapsed portion is the three-story wing on the right. First, the pointed roof and a large portion of the murals collapsed inward, and the two-story building below was crushed and collapsed as well. Fortunately, most of the staff and repair workers had already left, otherwise the death toll would have been much higher. The collapse was accompanied by a thunderous sound, and dust filled the sky. Tonight, the Vatican issued a statement saying that after inspecting the workers, none were injured, but students may have been harmed. The workers were working on the lowest level, repairing the walls. It is believed that the walls collapsed due to structural failure, causing the building to collapse. Although the library suffered significant damage in this accident, some books are expected to be intact. However, many treasures, such as murals, are irretrievably lost. The library was built in 1588 by Pope Sixtus V, and the walls and ceilings were painted by famous artists of the time. Vatican officials are currently on-site directing rescue efforts. It is said that the Pope had just left the library when the roof collapsed, only ten minutes earlier. Upon hearing that students were buried, the Pope knelt in prayer and personally visited the site. Reuters, Vatican City, 23rd – The bodies of Professor Fatazi and two workers were recovered from the library rubble overnight. It is feared that there are two or three more bodies. The upper level was the Hall of the Hundred Days, with walls painted by famous artists. Fortunately, it remains intact. The room contains items gifted by emperors and celebrities throughout history. A porcelain basin gifted by Napoleon was broken. The lower level was the consultation room, housing fifteen thousand paintings and extremely valuable texts, most of which are expected to be salvaged.

US Congress Adjourns for Holidays

Senate Approves Moratorium on War Debt Payments

National News, Washington, 22nd – The United States' Seventy-Second Congress adjourned today after three weeks of session, to recess for Christmas and New Year's holidays until January 4th of next year. The most important matter since Congress convened was the approval of President Hoover's plan to suspend war debt payments for one year. Other key matters, such as tax increases and budget proposals, will be revisited when Congress reconvenes next year.

Reuters, Washington, 22nd – The Senate today approved President Hoover's debt moratorium proposal by a vote of 69 to 12, and passed the House's amendment prohibiting any alteration or cancellation of war debts.

Vanguard Forces Pressing on Liuhugou

Aircraft Factory Under Construction in Xinmin County

Shenyang Communication: Since the anti-Japanese greenwoodsman White Dragon's unsuccessful attack on Shenyang on November 29th, the Japanese troops stationed in Qianjinzhai (i.e., Fushun) and Hicheng's Domon Unit have been transferred upon Benjo Shigeru's order. Moreover, gun emplacements were constructed on both the east and west banks of the Juluhe, and defensive fortifications were built nearby. Japan Plots to Buy the CER

France Sells CER Shares

Japan Secretly Seeks to Acquire

Russia States It Cannot Recognize

Harbin Communication: The secret compromise between France and Japan to jointly conspire against us has become an undeniable fact in recent events. Although the French troops are approaching the border of Guangdong, there have been no special movements. However, the news that Japan is accepting French shares in the Chinese Eastern Railway (CER) with the intention of buying the CER has become the most sensational piece of news here. According to local White Russian newspapers, the contract for the construction of the CER was signed between China and the Sino-Russian Bank (i.e., the Russo-Asiatic Bank). After the Russian Revolution, the majority of the Russo-Asiatic Bank's shares fell into the hands of France, some purchased by France, and some sold by Russians in the Meili market. In this way, the rights of the Russo-Asiatic Bank belong to France. The CER's railway property guarantees the Russo-Asiatic Bank's loans and serves as a commercial organization protecting French interests. In 1920, a new contract emerged between China and the Russo-Asiatic Bank. Since 1921, the Russo-Asiatic Bank has effectively become the owner of the CER's property. This was also recorded in the minutes of the Washington Conference that year. During the conference, Japan was entrusted to protect the rights of European countries in the CER. However, in 1924, the Feng-Soviet Agreement was reached, and Soviet Russia began jointly managing the CER with China, becoming a part-owner of the CER. All responsibilities to third parties were borne by the Soviet side. The Moscow Soviet government does not recognize any rights of France in the CER. At that time, Radkin, the Soviet Consul-General in Liaoning, issued a statement declaring that the CER shares were fictitious and that the railway belonged to the Russian Empire. The rights were accepted by the Soviet government and jointly owned with China. The Moscow government does not recognize any rights of France or any other third country in the CER. These expressions from the Russian consulate represent the opinion of its government. Therefore, since Soviet Russia and China jointly managed the railway, the rights of the Russo-Asiatic Bank completely disappeared. The bank subsequently went bankrupt. France and other countries that signed the Washington Conference protested to the Moscow government regarding this statement from the Soviet Union, especially France, which protested the most vehemently. However, due to inconsistent international circumstances at the time, the protests were unsuccessful, up until now. France has once again raised its rights in the CER. Influential newspapers in Paris have also published numerous articles discussing France's interests in the CER, advocating for France to take further actions to protect its rights. Financial and social circles have sent numerous letters to newspapers, calling for the restoration of France's rights in the CER. The French Consul, Lina, stationed in Harbin, was ordered by his government to make a detailed report on the current situation of the CER and the Sino-Russian cooperation. It is said that the French Consul stationed in Liaoning recently passed through Harbin on his way back to his country, which is related to this matter. Recently, French Consul Lina and Japanese Consul-General Tadaichi Ohashi met in Harbin, holding close discussions. Some say it was for this matter. However, the Soviet side does not acknowledge this, stating that even if France takes such actions, the Soviet Union will never recognize them as valid because the Soviet Union has long declared that the CER is jointly managed by China and Russia. Whether the shares scattered abroad are numerous or few, they have long ceased to be related to the railway. Russian Consul in Harbin, Bulunov, personally stated to the Harbin authorities yesterday that the Soviet Union cannot listen to the transfer of the CER. It is heard that the French side wants to sell the Harbin-Changchun line shares of the CER, while the Japanese side wants to obtain the Harbin-Changchun and Harbin-Manzhouli line shares, so they are still in negotiations. (18th)

Xi Qia Sends Personnel to Resolve the Wannbaoshan Incident

Overseen by the Pseudo-Changchun County Magistrate Zhao Rumei

With Japanese Participation, Led by Mr. Kuramoto, Staff Member of the Changchun Consulate

Harbin Communication: Since the Wannbaoshan Incident occurred on July 2nd, five months have passed in the blink of an eye. The Japanese invasion of our Northeast was essentially initiated by the Wannbaoshan Incident. Zhong Yu, the special envoy of the former Kuomintang Ministry of Foreign Affairs in Jilin, held negotiations with the Japanese Consul-General in Jilin, Ishimachi, in Jilin. However, due to the Japanese side's lack of sincerity, the negotiations came to a standstill. After the September 18th Incident occurred, the case was indefinitely shelved. Now, the Japanese believe that in this military occupation situation, if they use the puppet government of Jilin as the negotiating counterpart, they will be able to obtain the greatest benefits through negotiations. Therefore, they instructed Xi Qia, the pseudo-governor of Jilin, to order Jin Bi-dong, the chief of the Changchun Municipal Preparatory Office, to negotiate with the Japanese side in Changchun. In reality, this kind of negotiation is merely a formality. Of course, all conditions will comply with the Japanese side's intentions, so that the Japanese can obtain more practical guarantees for their rights to reside and lease land in our country's interior. However, according to rumors, Zhao Rumei believes that this case is of great importance. Although he has accepted the pseudo-order to negotiate, he is feigning compliance. Therefore, Kuramoto Hideaki has visited several times but has not been able to meet him. Is it possible that he still has a conscience? (17th)

After the Taiyuan Petition Tragedy

Industry and Commerce Halt Operations to Aid Students

School Principals Request Punishment of Responsible Personnel

Taiyuan dispatch: The Shanxi Provincial Student Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association, along with students from various schools, gathered at the Provincial Party Headquarters the day before yesterday (the 18th) to petition. They were shot at by the Party Headquarters' disciplinary team, leading to a tragic incident. Yesterday (the 19th) at 10:00 AM, all shops in the provincial capital closed down in solidarity with the students. Since the incident, the garrison headquarters has intensified surveillance of Party Headquarters personnel. The previous night, the 6th Company of the 400th Regiment was dispatched to garrison the Provincial Party Headquarters, and the 8th Company was dispatched to garrison the Municipal Party Headquarters. Liu Pingshun, the company commander of the 6th Company, stationed his troops in various departments and sections of the Party Headquarters, and detained 51 internal staff members in a room to prevent them from fleeing. However, the staff of the Municipal Party Headquarters all fled yesterday. According to investigations yesterday morning, the number of injured students has increased again, with several having their spines broken, potentially leading to disability. Two students, a Mr. Li from No. 1 Middle School and a Mr. Zhang from a mountain school, remain missing. After the Student Union reported this to the Public Security Bureau, Director Wang Xifu, along with Section Chief Yang of the 3rd Section and Bureau Officer Qiao from the 4th Branch of the Bureau, and two representatives from the Student Union, led police officers to the Provincial Party Headquarters at 9:00 AM yesterday to search the wells. They only recovered two willow dippers. To investigate the perpetrators, the Student Union has stationed disciplinary teams at each city gate since yesterday to strictly check for wanted criminals. They have also deployed personnel at train and bus stations to prevent escapes. They will cooperate with the police and military police to conduct household registrations and search for criminals within the next few days. Personnel have also been stationed in front of the Pu Xin Bookstore. It has been decided that a memorial service for Mu Guangzheng will be held at Zhongshan Park at 1:00 PM this afternoon (the 20th). Workers will cease work for one day, and newspapers will suspend publication for one day. Yesterday morning, principals of secondary and higher schools held a meeting at Shanxi University to discuss measures to assist regarding this tragedy. They immediately drafted two petitions to be submitted to the Provincial Government, expressing their opinions. The petitions are recorded below: (1) Upon investigation, the student anti-Japanese national salvation movement has occurred in this province following the events in Beiping, Shanghai, and Wuhan. At that time, the principals followed the orders of the Central Government and the government to try to stop it, but unfortunately, the youth of the city, motivated by righteous indignation, were temporarily unsuccessful, resulting in the events of the 11th of this month. The principals are responsible for their duties and bear the blame. They are continuing to persuade and find ways to resume classes, but yesterday there was a sudden unprecedented tragedy in this city. The important goal of the Student Union's Anti-Japanese Association's petition is to remove the Director of Education, Miao. At this time, Director Miao should personally avoid taking action, and the government should present this matter to the Central Government and resolve it as soon as possible to avoid further unpredictable events. The principals are worried and cannot remain silent. In addition to continuing to stop the students, they should jointly submit a written request for review and implementation. (2) The student patriotic movement in this province followed the national movement, resulting in a conflict with the education authorities. The principals have repeatedly tried to stop it before and after the fact, but they were powerless and things went against their wishes, resulting in the tragic killing incident on the 18th of this month. The principals deeply regret the situation. However, this incident involved students who are ignorant youths, motivated by patriotic enthusiasm, and there were no excessive actions. However, representatives were beaten and the masses were bombed, resulting in several deaths and injuries. This kind of brutal behavior deserves punishment. The government should swiftly transfer the perpetrators to the court for strict punishment according to the law, in order to comfort the young people who died unjustly. (December 20th)

Another dispatch from Taiyuan: Yesterday (the 18th), the Student Union Anti-Japanese Association held a large anti-Japanese propaganda rally in Zhongshan Park. Approximately 3,000 students attended. Disciplinary teams formed by famous schools all carried wooden sticks. The garrison troops and public security bureau's security team were also present to suppress the rally. After representatives from various schools spoke about the violent occupation of Northeast China by Japan and the current turmoil in this province, they formed a procession to march. At the same time, approximately 500 workers from the Huochai Company, Jinsheng Factory, and Pingmin Factory gathered on Jingying Street, also carrying wooden sticks and shouting slogans. These workers were directed by the Provincial Party Headquarters and almost clashed with the students. However, because there were many people from all sides, they were mutually persuaded. After the unfortunate incident, the Provincial and Municipal Party Headquarters sent troops to protect the area. Around 12:00 PM, all the students went to the Provincial Party Headquarters to petition, demanding that a telegram be sent to the Central Government to dismiss and punish Director of Education Miao Peicheng, and to support the students in rising up to resist Japan. At that time, they shouted slogans such as "Support Wang Jingwei," "Down with Japanese Imperialism," "Down with the Communist Party," and "Down with Miao Peicheng, who obstructs the Anti-Japanese Movement." Upon hearing the news, the Provincial Party Headquarters mobilized the disciplinary team and the militia formed by various officials of the Provincial and Municipal Party Headquarters, using live ammunition to block the main gate, preventing the students from entering. After tens of minutes of arguing, a certain regimental commander maintaining order smoothed things over with a member of the Provincial Executive Committee, who sent more than 20 representatives to enter. After the representatives entered the gate, they saw that the disciplinary team and the militia of the Provincial Party Headquarters were fully armed, lined up on both sides, with guns and wooden sticks arranged like a dense forest, creating a sense of fear. They went to the conference room, where Han Kewen, Yao Dahai, Su Shouyu, and Li Min received them. The representatives stated the purpose of their petition. Han and others said that it could not be decided by a few people and would be answered after an emergency meeting was convened to discuss it. The representatives left and informed all the students. Everyone believed that the reply was not to the point and asked the representatives to negotiate again. After the representatives entered the second time, they saw that everything was different from before. The conference room's doorway and windows were completely surrounded by disciplinary teams, creating a solemn atmosphere. After the representatives entered the conference room, the four committee members, Han and the others, left. Two minutes later, the disciplinary team and the militia burst in. The representatives, seeing that the situation was not good, intended to reason with them, but gunshots and wooden sticks were heard in succession. The representatives were unable to avoid them and had nowhere to hide. Fortunately, Su Shouyu entered the room and ordered the disciplinary team to stop. The representatives were about to take the opportunity to withdraw, but after walking about a dozen steps, the disciplinary team in front blocked the way, and the disciplinary team behind chased after them. The militia on the east and west sides also crowded in from the sides. Because the gate was locked, the representatives could not escape, and gunshots and wooden sticks fell like wind and rain. As the representatives retreated into the conference room, the disciplinary team and the militia chased them on all sides. This happened three times. The disciplinary team also chased

Page 10

The representatives huddled at the gate, and saw a small hole in the wooden door on the side, through which one could enter and exit. Therefore, they urgently crawled out through this door. However, because the hole was as small as a bottle, it took several minutes to escape one person. As a result, more than 20 representatives were beaten by wooden sticks and almost none escaped unscathed. When the entire student body heard the news, they swarmed forward, shouting to hit, and threw stones randomly, hoping to break through the door to rescue the representatives. However, the disciplinary team guarding the gate immediately opened fire. Gunshots rang out, and the students all fled to the entrance of the Grain Bureau to Shang Xiao. Nearby residents were also panicked. After the garrison commander heard the report, he led three battalions of garrison troops to suppress the situation, and at the students' request, completely disarmed the disciplinary team and militia, confiscating a total of 58 rifles, 12 submachine guns, and 3 pistols. Subsequently, the Provincial Executive Committee members Han, Yao Dahai, Su Shouyu, and Li Min, and the militia were escorted to the garrison headquarters by car. The disarmed disciplinary team was sent to the 10th Gendarmerie Team. The Provincial and Municipal Party Headquarters were closed that night by the garrison commander, gendarmerie, and public security bureau, and a battalion of troops was stationed inside. (December 19th)

Guangzhou Students Petition to Resist Japan

Five Requests to the Guangdong Government Accepted

Guangzhou dispatch: Because the provincial five schools recently petitioned the government to send troops, but did not get satisfactory results, the student community convened the entire city's students again on the 17th to hold a large petition. On that day, students from various schools gathered in the Yuexiu Sports Field one after another, beginning at 10 a.m. Participants included students from Lingnan University, National University, Sun Yat-sen University, Guangzhou University, School of Law, School of Political Science and Law, Zhiyong Middle School, Girls' Middle School, Guanghua Middle School, Panyu Normal School, Pui Ching Middle School, First Middle School, Dazhong Middle School, Dongshan Middle School, Municipal Women's Vocational School, Kunwei Girls' School, Zhixing Middle School, Lingqiao Girls' School, Journalism School, Municipal First Middle School, Provincial Second Middle School, Physical Education School, Nanjing Middle School, Shiyan Middle School, Women's Normal School, Nursing School, Pui To, Pui Ying, Municipal Second Middle School, Xinghua School, Jiaozhong Normal School, Zhongkai School, Zhixin School, Guanghan School, Tuqiang School, Guanghua Medical School, Municipal Art School, First Normal School, Shiyan Middle School, Baosheng School, etc., totaling over 10,000 students. At noon, they lined up and went to the National Government. Chen Wenzao, a representative from Sun Yat-sen University, served as the temporary student commander. Upon arriving in front of the National Government, Chen Wenzao and eight others were elected as representatives to submit a petition with five requests: (1) Please appoint a general supervisor of student volunteer military training for the entire city immediately, and issue firearms and personnel to train rescue teams in various schools, and issue protective supplies. (2) Please send troops to recover lost territory immediately. (3) Please send a Guangdong Central Committee member north immediately to organize a unified government. (4) Please issue a clear order to allow absolute freedom for the student national salvation movement. (5) Please investigate and handle the officials who ordered the guards to shoot and kill the petitioning students from the five provincial schools, take photos of the officials, and publish apologies in newspapers in Guangdong, Hong Kong, Beijing, and Shanghai. Xiang Hanping received the representatives. Xiang's reply was as follows: "The National Government is currently planning to appoint He Tong as the general supervisor of student training. Students who are well-trained can be issued guns immediately. If they have not been trained, they must wait for six months of training before they can be issued weapons. As for the current situation, troops can only be sent to resist Japan after a unified government is established. The government can approve the other requests." The students replied verbally, and still demanded that the above five points be answered in writing. Xiang then entered the National Government and consulted with the authorities, immediately convening a meeting to discuss it. At 2:00 p.m., Xiang came out again and gave the students a written reply to the five requests as follows: (1) He Tong is appointed as the general supervisor of the Guangzhou city student military training. After the New Year's Day general review of the student volunteer military forces in the city, firearms will be issued separately within a week. Before New Year's Day, personnel will be dispatched separately to train rescue teams in various schools and issue protective supplies. (2) Immediately mobilize all armies and prepare to set off, and ask representatives of each school to go to Nanjing to petition first, and allow our army to pass. If there is no response, send a telegram to Guangdong requesting that troops be sent immediately. If the National Government still fails to send troops at that time, students can overthrow the Guangdong government. (3) All members of the Central Committee will go to Hong Kong on the 17th and transfer to Shanghai by ship on the 18th to go to Nanjing to organize a unified government. (4) A clear order will be announced before the 19th. (5) By the 20th of this month at the latest, an order will be issued to dismiss the officials who insulted the students, take photos of the officials, and publish apologies in newspapers in Guangdong, Hong Kong, Beijing, and Shanghai. The students were satisfied and temporarily moved that the government allocate travel expenses for student representatives if they went north. Xiang agreed to ask the government to allocate them. At this point, the student representatives began to shout slogans and withdrew. It was already 5:00 p.m. (December 27th)

Jinan Petitioning Students Return

Jinan dispatch: The Jinan City students petitioning delegation to Beijing (2,572 students from 13 schools) returned north from Pukou by two trains on the morning of the 18th and arrived in Jinan this morning (the 20th). Students and faculty members from various schools who stayed behind came to the station to welcome them. Various labor unions also sent representatives in teams holding flags to express their welcome. The Department of Education, the Municipal Government, and the Public Security Bureau also sent personnel to the station to take care of the situation. At 9:30 a.m., the first train arrived at the station carrying students from high schools and Yuying schools. At 10:30 a.m., the second train arrived carrying students from the remaining ten schools. The entire group lined up to get off the train. The delegation, holding flags, led the way, and the rest followed in order on the platform. According to delegation standing committee member Li Xiujie, when talking to reporters, the delegation initially believed that this movement was extremely significant, but when students from various places held a general demonstration in Beijing on the 17th, due to the complexity of the elements, the resolution of the general assembly of representatives was overturned. Therefore, the Jinan students did not participate in the general demonstration that day, not out of greed for life or fear of death, but because Chairman Jiang had stepped down and the government had no officially responsible person, so bloodshed was not worth it. However, as soon as they heard about the tragedy that day, they immediately sent a team to help, resulting in the arrest of two people (Li Henian from the First Rural Normal School and Fu Weiya from the First Vocational School, who have now been bailed out). The students felt that petitioning the government was meaningless, so they decided to return to Jinan to do their best to awaken the mass movement and universally spread anti-Japanese national salvation. This ambition and this heart will never slacken and cannot be dispelled by any force. The delegation had a total of three thousand five hundred and seventy-two people when it left, more than ten people became ill on the way, more than one hundred were persuaded to return by the principals to Beijing, and two were arrested. Today, three thousand two hundred and ninety-seven people returned to Jinan. At 11:00 a.m., Labor Union representative Yan Tianle delivered a welcoming speech to the students. Student representative Li Huanlun delivered a reply. After the speeches, they shouted slogans, formed a procession, and left the station to parade. The propaganda team led the way, distributing propaganda. They marched southeast from the Jinpu Station, passing through Dama Road, turning south, passing through Jingwei First Road, turning east to Erma Road, entering Puli Gate, passing through Puli Street, Guyi Market Street, to Daxi Gate, passing through Ximen Dajie, turning north, passing through Anchasi Street, turning east to the Department of Education. Because it was Sunday, no one was there to meet them. They also went to the Provincial Party Headquarters, but no one was there to meet them because it was Sunday, so they all dispersed and returned to their schools. (December 20th)

Niu Yongjian Resigns as Minister of Personnel

Niu Yongjian, Minister of Personnel, submitted a report to the National Government, stating: "I, Yongjian, was originally a scholar. In the late Qing Dynasty, seeing the decline of the country, I abandoned literature and learned martial arts, determined to devote myself to the revolution. Following the pioneers, I devoted myself to military affairs for more than thirty years, daring not to slacken. Since the National Revolutionary Army established the capital, I have been favored by the Party and the country and have held important civil posts. After several years of following the routine, I know that I have made mistakes. I had long ago made the decision to retire. I was repeatedly retained by clear orders, and it was a time of national crisis, so I did not dare to ask to return. Now, the violent Japanese are showing their ferocity and occupying our three provinces without cause. The whole country is rushing to face the difficulties. Our cooperation has promoted unity, which has been realized. I, Yongjian, am accustomed to military life, and have long prepared for military service. I was not cut out for politics, and offering my services was my original intention. At this time when the national policy has been set and the threat of invasion has not ceased, it is not appropriate to hold a position without performing my duties and going against my heart. I dare to express my feelings and earnestly request that you approve my resignation from the current position as Minister of Personnel, so that I may devote my modest efforts to the work of resisting foreign aggression. If the Party and the country believe that there is still a place where Yongjian can be of service, whether at the front or in the rear, I am willing to defend the country with a weapon in hand and dare not refuse any difficulty. I humbly submit this report and await your orders."

After questioning Ji Sitang, Zhou stated that on the night of the theft, seven or eight people who sounded like guests entered the house at 7 p.m. The ninth person was Ji Sitang, who was arrested. Ji Sitang did not say a word when he entered, but Zhou clearly identified him. Yesterday, when Zhou was shopping in Sijing, he recognized the person, so he handed him over to the police. Ji Sitang stated that he lived in Zhao Shitu and was currently working for Shen Maosheng. He joined the store in August. Yesterday, he was arrested by the woman for no reason. His brother, Zhu Huanrong, submitted a statement to defend him, but it did not match Ji Sitang's statement. Since the case involves robbery, Ji Sitang and Zhou Bosheng were sent to the county government and then to the county court for trial.

Repair the ring road and widen the three main roads. The Suzhou City Xiagang Road, from Pingmen to Tu Jin Xu Pan to Da Yinmen Midu Bridge, is about 8,000 meters long. It has not been repaired for more than 20 years. The Construction Bureau plans to repair it in the original style. Manholes and pipes will be laid in the prosperous commercial areas. It will be submitted to the Construction Department for approval today and work will begin immediately. The Construction Bureau plans to widen the three main roads of Lindun Road, Gongxiang, and East-West Zhongshi. The survey has been completed and was also submitted to the Department for approval yesterday.

The party affairs dispute expands. Unexpectedly, at 4 p.m. that afternoon, Ji Pu, a former member of the county party committee who had already resigned, and Gan Ciqing, a secretary, took the county police team and the Public Security Bureau's special police to arrest people in various places. This continued until 3 a.m. this morning (23), when Mao Junbai and the other six were released. Jiangyin

Qian Nanyun's rape case opens for trial. Qian Nanyun, the principal of the Qingyang Temple Elementary School in the 11th district, was reported for raping Liu Xiufeng, a 12-year-old female student at the school, by her father, Liu Guifang, to the Qingyang Public Security Second Branch and sent to the General Bureau for transfer to the county for trial. Qian was detained in the Public Security Bureau Detention Center. Because his cotton pants and lining pants had semen stains, he was exchanged with Huang Qi, a police officer on duty, but was noticed by a patrol officer, who presented the pants to the county. After Qian was sent to the county, he took the opportunity to urinate and tried to escape by climbing the wall. The judicial police reported to the county. At 4 p.m., Magistrate Ma conducted a secret trial. First, Liu Guifang explained the process, and then Liu Qifeng was interrogated, who stated that she had been raped by Mr. Qian Nanyun, causing a lot of bleeding in her lower body. Qian Nanyun stated that he graduated from the Third Normal School in the 17th year and had been the principal of the Miaoqian Elementary School for two years. There were 38 male students and 5 female students. Each semester there were 100 yuan for tuition and board. He went home on Thursday, and the blood on his pants was caused by his wife's menstruation. He did not admit to raping Xiufeng and did not admit to trying to escape out of fear of crime. Then Liu Xiufeng confronted him to prove it. Qian was evasive. Magistrate Ma carefully examined the diagnosis from Fuyin Hospital. Xiufeng had injuries, tears in the vulva, perineum, and vaginal opening, and the hymen was also torn. There was no bleeding at the present time and it did not endanger her life. Based on the above evidence, Qian's rape of the female student was undeniable. After the interrogation, his wife, Hu, was brought in for questioning, but the answers did not match. When asked by the interrogator, Qian admitted to the rape and asked for a lenient sentence. After the interrogation, he was taken into custody pending sentencing.

Negotiation on occupation of civilian land for the automobile road. After the Xicheng long-distance automobile road was opened, the Construction Bureau has not yet measured the land price tax for the occupation of civilian land. The Finance Bureau has exempted the tax. The township heads and deputies of Qinnan Township held a meeting the other day. Yin Xi Shen proposed that no price had been given for the occupation of civilian land, and the land price tax was still paid by the original owner. What kind of negotiation should be adopted? (1) The district head of the district should send a letter to the Construction Bureau and the Automobile Company, stating that before the government has completed the procedures for issuing the land price and exempting the land price tax, the automobile should be temporarily suspended to prevent accidents. (2) The landowners should contact each other and organize a negotiation committee. (3) The township heads, deputies, and township affairs council secretaries along the route should be the negotiators.

Changzhou

Fire at Shanghai Hoji Match Factory. The former Zhensheng Electric Light Factory near Huangxing outside Xiaonanmen in Wuyi was leased to the Shanghai Hoji Match Factory last year. The factory began production in March of this year. The factory originally had a capital of 60,000 yuan, but only 10,000 yuan was raised. The shareholders were Wang Zihe and others, and the manager was Chuan Kanghui. After boycotting Japanese goods, due to the lack of raw materials and the accumulation of inventory, the factory had been closed for three months. Unexpectedly, yesterday (22) at 2:00 p.m., a fire suddenly broke out. All the machines and workshops for making matches, a total of 16 rooms, and more than 400 boxes of matches were burned to ashes. The loss was estimated to be more than 20,000 yuan. The electric motors of the electric light factory were also damaged, and the value was also high. The cause of the fire was said to be due to excessive pressure from the piled-up goods.

Lake bandits loot and kidnap people on Jiaoshan. Recently, a large group of lake bandits in Taihu Lake, on two large fishing boats, anchored near Jiaoshan, and have been looting small fishing boats for several days. They have also kidnapped Xu Rongda and are heading towards Sanshan. The news today (23) is that the victims and nearby residents have reported to the Ma Jishan water police stationed there, who will send patrol boats to search and suppress the bandits in the lake.

Statistics on Japanese goods sealed up in the provincial capital. The Association has now sent personnel to conduct a detailed investigation to understand the amount and value of the sealed goods. A written report has been submitted to the Provincial Party Headquarters for verification.

When Cheng was appointed to the Jiangsu Department of Education, he had resolved to resign, but he has not yet taken office. As a result, the Jiangsu Department of Education is in a state of no one in charge. The staff are idle all day, and there are many important documents piled up. The staff in the Department are eager for Cheng to come to the province and make some arrangements to avoid this prolonged stagnation.

Relief for the lost wheat. The National Government Disaster Relief Association has set up a grain station in Tongzhou. The boat loaded with Zhen Mai was lost in the wind a few days ago. The Association has sent Shen Chusheng and Wang Weixin to Tongzhou to investigate and deal with the aftermath. The loss is estimated to be 490 bags of American wheat. The bodies of five drowned crew members, including Tao Xuekun, have been recovered. Five Jiang boats have been found, all of which have been damaged. The remaining six boats have been labeled and are being searched for in the Quanhu, Pulong, and Liuhe areas.

The truth about the disaster in the county. The Nantong County Government recently investigated the truth about the disaster in the county and reported it to the province. It is estimated that 350 square li out of the county's 7,440 square li had no harvest at all, and 800 square li had less than 30% harvest. There were 227,348 disaster-stricken households with 1,108,461 people. The disaster in the east township was particularly severe, and the victims were living on vegetable roots.

County Party Headquarters increases security. The County Party Headquarters recently sent a letter to the County Government requesting the deployment of military police to increase security to prevent accidents, as there were rumors that someone was plotting to sabotage the headquarters.

Education News

Special Article

Resistance Against Japan and Military Training (Wang Geng)

The solution after resistance against Japan is a military solution. The purpose of military training is to ensure that all people have military knowledge and skills. The ultimate goal is to consolidate national defense. Now the Training Supervision Department has issued a notice to all secondary schools and above in the country to intensify military training. This is indeed a fundamental way for young people to save the country. However, attention should be paid to the basic understanding of those receiving training. The author has been involved in this field for several years and knows a thing or two about its shortcomings. Now, in the midst of the nationwide call for resistance against Japan and the intensified military training of young people, I would like to offer my humble opinion to the national education community and young people.

First, Have an Ideology. The success of Mr. Sun Yat-sen's revolution was due to the Three Principles of the People. No matter how big or small a thing is, it will never be successful without an ideology. Military training without an ideology will certainly create a useless army. In the Russo-Japanese War, the Japanese had the ideology of avenging their shame, so they were able to defeat Russia in one battle. In the French Revolution, the soldiers all embraced the ideology of freedom and equality, and despite decades of bloody battles, they still achieved final success. Similarly, American soldiers have the Monroe Doctrine, Japanese troops have the Greater East Asia Doctrine, and German troops have the overseas colonial doctrine. Whether their ideologies are right or wrong is another question. We should know that an ideology is a must. Our military training should be based on the ideology of saving the country, or rather, the ideology of resistance.

Second, Have a Common Enemy. An army must have a common enemy. With a common enemy, the soldiers will be brave and invincible. For example, in the Franco-Prussian War of 1870, the French common enemy was Germany. After the Sino-Japanese War, Japan's common enemy was Russia. After the European War, America's common enemy was Japan. They always envision how the common enemy will be in their daily military training in order to prepare for war. Our military training should also have a common enemy. Who is the common enemy? It is Japan and the great powers.

Third, Be Strict and Obedient. The strength of an army has two types: one is tangible strength, such as the number of soldiers and horses, and the sharpness of weapons; the other is intangible strength, such as strict discipline, obedience, and bravery. Intangible strength is very important in determining the size of combat power. There are many historical examples of an army with this intangible strength being able to defeat the enemy. In the Wuchang Uprising, the leader was a platoon leader named Xiong Bingkun with only thirty-one bullets, yet he captured the city of Wuchang. Just imagine, thirty-two bullets, even if one bullet kills one person, would only kill thirty-two people. This was entirely due to the intangible strength. Therefore, military training should absolutely eliminate all romantic and casual habits.

Fourth, Be Able to Endure Hardship. Since the purpose of military training is to consolidate national defense, the future war will be with foreigners, not with our own Chinese people. There will be no convenience in fighting foreigners like in a civil war. A military expert once told me that in the future, fighting foreigners will probably not be like running forward in a civil war, but crawling forward. Because of the power of telegraphs and artillery fire, it will be impossible to stand upright and move forward. Airplanes will drop bombs from the air, so defense will require living in trenches. How can a person without the ability to endure hardship survive in this situation? Therefore, when we receive military training, we should resolve to embrace the spirit of enduring hardship.

The above four points are all fundamental requirements for an army. Young people, do you believe me? Please wake up quickly and put them into practice for the sake of the country! (Written at Wuxi Education College)

After Visiting the Patriotic Activities Achievement Competition Fair - Zhang Angqian

There have been many competitions, but the Patriotic Activities Achievement Competition Fair held by the Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau is probably its pioneering work. It is based on the observation that the so-called patriotism and education to save the country are not necessarily mutually supportive. Talking about education, it seems that the meaning of patriotism is completely contained within. Talking about patriotism, education is often seen as a slow and ineffective plan. The mistakes of the past are so great that we must have today's awareness to learn from the past. Where does the awareness come from? In China, where the enemy is deep and the disaster is urgent, although education has no national boundaries, if we want to resist insults and save the country, we must follow the Prime Minister's nationalism and take patriotism as the center of implementing the Three Principles of the People. To observe the past achievements of various schools in patriotic education and to indicate and inspire the future direction of efforts of various schools, the Patriotic Activities Achievement Competition Fair is still admired. Therefore, it is known that this fair is not only a need to adapt to the current environment, but also cannot be compared with ordinary competitions. The mission and significance of the fair are uniquely great and tragic. After the visit, I have some feelings, and I write them down as follows: (A) In terms of planning, the implementation plan of patriotic activities in Danhua, the implementation outline of patriotic activity center education in He'an, and the current affairs education in the national crisis in Luhu, (divided into) (1) Today's classroom, (2) Newspaper education, (3) National crisis current affairs, (4) Clear goals, (5) Teaching time, (6) Selection of pen and paper, (7) Scope of materials, (8) Newspaper reading guidance, (9) Opportunity giving, (10) Instance contribution, (11) Teacher reference, (12) (Conclusion,) are relatively thorough and appropriate.

(B) In terms of teaching, the teaching outline of the Northeast Incident in Qimei and the research outline of patriotic activity center education in He'an are both suitable for the main points.

(C) In terms of teaching materials, such as the teaching materials for the low-grade group of Jiancheng School, (Little friends, you must know that a piece of candy, a bag of fruit, bought to eat, not full, save some money, build guns and cannons, Japanese slaves overthrow the country) and the self-compiled teaching materials of Shanghai Private Elementary School (A short man in a Taoist robe, a short woman in a nun's robe, a short child, neither monk nor Taoist) (2) (The beautiful cherry blossom is the national flower of the Japanese, but the cherry blossom is not as good as the plum blossom, Great China, not afraid of the small three islands,) are worthy of being clear and appropriate. The supplementary teaching materials for each subject in Dui De School are also very commendable.

(D) In terms of student achievements, the competition results of each subject in Xicheng, the test results of Wan Zhu's Yu Chan, the comparison of important commercial ports and ports in Northeast China and the armament of China, Japan, and the world, the results of children's spontaneous activity in He'an, various current affairs tests, the publication of children's weekly newspapers, the survey form of domestic and Japanese goods, and the results of each subject in Zhenxiu show that there are a large number of student products.

Middle School Students Discuss Resuming Classes Without Results

A Dispute Arises Between Mingqiang and Anmo's

The Shanghai Secondary School Students' Anti-Japanese National Salvation Federation held its 11th plenary representative meeting at Qingxin Middle School on Lujiabang Road, Ximen, at 10 a.m. yesterday. Representatives from 47 schools, totaling over a hundred people, attended. The chairman, Li Bin of Huijian Middle School, immediately began to

discuss the issue of resuming classes. Some representatives advocated reconsideration, while others unanimously insisted on waiting for the demonstration group to return to Shanghai from Beijing before resuming classes. There was a fierce debate between those who supported and those who opposed resuming classes, and the atmosphere was very tense. The discussion continued from 10 a.m. to 1 p.m. without any results. While the meeting was in progress, Sun Zihe, a representative of Mingqiang Middle School students at Anmo's Girls' Middle School, reported that the school authorities had issued a notice to all students yesterday, ordering them to attend classes immediately, otherwise the supply of electricity, water, and food would be stopped, and they also demanded that the anti-Japanese associations of both schools be disbanded at the same time, otherwise they would be expelled from the school. Yesterday, the Student Federation sent Fang Zhou and Li Bin to investigate. As a result, the students resolved to petition to attend classes in order to avoid disputes and requested that the authorities not interfere with the anti-Japanese work. However, their request was not granted, and the students were extremely angry and reconsidered continuing the strike. According to Li Bin, the chairman of the Secondary School Student Federation, both schools were founded by the American Christian Baptist Church, and although they are called two schools, they have the same principal, Li Haoshan. This morning, he ordered all students to leave the school and cut off all supplies. The conference resolved to send a hundred volunteers to maintain order.

Fang Xuanzhou, a representative of Dongwu No. 2 Middle School, reported that the school authorities had ordered the students to resume classes immediately and requested that the students respond before 2 p.m. today (i.e., yesterday). He asked the conference to consider this and stated that if the association had no ability to provide assistance, the school would have no choice but to withdraw from the Student Federation and compromise. The conference representatives immediately went to various schools to investigate and negotiate.

According to Xin Sheng News Agency, when the Secondary School Anti-Japanese National Salvation Federation held a representative conference at Qingxin Middle School yesterday morning, representatives from Mingqiang and Anmo's schools reported that the two schools were forcing students to leave the school and had decided to stop supplying water, electricity, and food this afternoon (i.e., yesterday), otherwise the students would have to resume classes unconditionally. The school also reported to the Public Security Bureau, asking them to dispatch officers to the school to suppress the students for not maintaining order. The Public Security Bureau has dispatched over twenty police officers to the school to monitor the situation. Please send personnel to assist. Upon receiving the report, the Student Federation immediately dispatched volunteers from Qingxin, Quanzhang, and Gongshi schools to the rescue. Because the volunteers from Quanzhang all had fake firearms, they were unable to pass through the concession. Therefore, they sent a small number of personnel, unarmed, to Mingqiang and Anmo's schools to maintain order and rescue the forced students. At around 3 p.m., the representatives of various schools who were attending the conference in Qingxin went to Mingqiang and Anmo's schools. For a time, the disciplinary team, volunteers, and representatives such as Yu Xi were all over the two schools, and they monitored the telephones to prevent external actions. After the representatives of each school arrived, they held a representative conference in the auditorium of Mingqiang to continue discussing countermeasures. The following resolutions were passed: (1) The school shall not interfere with students' patriotic movement. (2) The school authorities shall not prevent students from complying with all resolutions of the Student Federation. (3) The Student Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association shall not be dissolved under any pretext. (4) Anti-Japanese association officers shall not be dismissed under any pretext. (5) A memorial week for the Premier must be held with fifteen articles that must be required for Ming An two schools to effectively recognize, the conference elected representatives Jiao Cai Xian and others to negotiate with the president, but because the president was not present, only to be flat-handed to the director of the Department of Li Xingxian to answer on behalf of said that I was in charge of teaching affairs, can only implement all matters related to teaching affairs, for the school's major events, can not be responsible on behalf of the reply. Passes the Draft Constitution of the Association

Inaugural Meeting to be Held on the 28th

The United Association of Faculty and Staff of Universities in the city, after the previous preparatory committee nominated Kang Xuanyi, Wang Zaoshi, Shi Ting, and others to draft the constitution and declaration of the association, has now completed the draft and convened the second preparatory committee meeting at the Hua An Insurance Company at 4:30 pm yesterday to discuss it. The details of the meeting are as follows:

Attendees: Hu Shuhua, Zheng Hongnian, Zhang Shouyong, Li Zhaoshi, Kang Xuanyi, Wang Zaoshi, He Tingshu, Lin Zhongke, Jiang Zhensan, Chu Minyi, (Nong Ruyu represented Li Bangdong, Zheng Hongnian was elected chairman, and Li Bangdong recorded the minutes.

Passing the Constitution: The draft constitution of the Shanghai University Faculty and Staff Association was passed as follows: 1. Name: The name of this association is the Shanghai University Faculty and Staff Association. 2. Purpose: The purpose of this association is to connect emotions, research academics, promote culture, and cultivate national strength. 3. Nature: This association has the nature of a social, academic, and professional group. 4. Membership: Any faculty and staff working in registered schools above the undergraduate level in Shanghai may become members of this association. 5. The meetings of this association are divided into the following categories: (A) General membership meeting: at least twice per semester. If necessary, a temporary meeting may be convened upon the proposal of 20 or more members or the resolution of the executive committee and the representative meeting. (B) Representative meeting: at least once per month. (C) Executive committee and supervisory committee: once every two weeks. Temporary meetings may be convened when necessary. (D) Other committee meetings: determined by each committee. 6. The representative meeting of this association is organized by the following two types of representatives. Detailed rules of procedure will be formulated separately. A. School representatives: Two representatives from each university, one representative from each independent college and specialty. The term of office for representatives is one year. B. Member representatives: 30 people, elected by the general meeting. The term of office is half a year and can be re-elected. 7. The executive committee of this association consists of 15 people, and the supervisory committee consists of 5 people, elected by the workers' congress. Representatives can also serve as committee members. Committee members do not have to be representatives. The term of office is one year. 8. The executive committee members may establish various specialized committees at any time and hire members to take charge of various association affairs. Detailed rules of procedure will be formulated separately. 9. The executive committee will mutually elect five standing committee members to handle daily affairs. 10. The expenses are divided into the following categories: A. Membership fee: 20 to 50 yuan per school, 2 yuan per person, payable upon joining the association. B. Regular expenses: 20 to 50 yuan per school per month, 1 yuan per person per year. C. Special donations: solicited by the executive committee members upon the resolution of the representative meeting. 11. The location of this association is in Shanghai. 12. The quorum for various meetings of this association is more than half of the total number of people in each meeting. 13. These regulations may be amended by a proposal submitted by 20 or more members and passed by the general membership meeting. 14. These regulations will take effect after being resolved by the general membership meeting, and the inaugural meeting will be held at the Youth Association at 10:00 am on the 28th of this month (Sunday) to pass the declaration and constitution of the association.

Zhu Lunda Returns to China After Completing His Studies

Mr. Zhu Lunda returned to China from the United States yesterday. Mr. Zhu once served as a guiding committee member and executive committee member of the Kuomintang Philadelphia branch in the United States, vice president of the Pacific Northwest Federation of the International Student Friendship Conference in the United States, and won the first prize in the English declamation competition at the 1929 annual meeting of the Chinese Students Association in the western United States, and the 1929 Wenner Peace Essay Award from Curry College in the United States. He graduated from Curry College in the same year with a Bachelor of Political Science degree. Last year, he served as a lecturer at Curry College. This year, he graduated from the University of California with a Master of Science in Transportation Management.
