Page 11

Talking about Freedom

Random Thoughts of Dai Liang

— Yan Zi

Su Shi of the Song Dynasty had a passion for inkstones. He possessed many fine pieces. By today's era, almost none remain. Currently, those who are renowned for collecting inkstones are Xu Xiuzhi and Lin Baishui. However, Lin's collection is far less extensive and exquisite than Xu's. Xu is known throughout the country as the owner of the Hundred Inkstone Studio. It is said that he has acquired renowned inkstones such as the Banana Leaf White Jade with Yellow Duan Blood Silk Orchid Pavilion Residual Stone Inkstone at great expense. His deep passion for inkstones is evident. However, after Lin Baishui passed away, most of his inkstone collection was acquired by the Japanese. Only two large Qinghua ice-pattern inkstones remain in China. Xu feared that these would also be purchased by the Japanese, so he repeatedly asked people to plead with Lin's descendants to sell them to him. He has already acquired the Qinghua ice-pattern inkstones. He held a banquet in the Hundred Inkstone Studio, inviting Wang Fuan, Qin Gangsun, He Tianjian, and others to evaluate them. They all praised them highly. The so-called ice patterns resemble drooping willow branches, with a beautiful color. They are rare and precious inkstones that are unmatched in modern times. After discussions, it was decided that Xu would purchase them to prevent them from flowing into the three islands of Japan. Each person composed a poem on the spot to commemorate the occasion. By the time the banquet ended, it was already past midnight.

Chats in Buting Study

How Can One Avoid Being a Relic of the Past?

Reply to a Letter from a Young Elementary School Teacher

...Reading your letter, I am so gratified to know that you aspire to make progress! If we don't want to be relics of the past, we must specialize in a natural science. Natural science is the express train to the ideal world. Stay on board and you will never be left behind. I now plan to devote the rest of my life to specializing in a science. Let's ride this train together! From agricultural civilization to industrial civilization, natural science is the only bridge. Elementary school teachers must hold the torch of science to guide children through the transition. Those who do not understand science will soon be unable to teach. But there is one thing you must keep in mind: science has been used by butchers as a weapon to kill. We must seize science from the hands of the butchers. We must teach students to use science to help people cross, not to use science to prevent people from crossing. We must use science to suppress the strong and support the weak. The mission of science is to create a wealthy society, not wealthy individuals. Before natural science becomes a national product, we must master a foreign language to acquire the latest knowledge and methods in natural science. These are all things you need to recognize and prepare for. Come and let's talk in detail!...

Going to War

— A Member of the First Youth Support-Horse Team

(7) Leaving Wuxi

The lemon-colored sun hangs obliquely on the distant treetops. It was probably a little past five o'clock at this time. The train car was still rushing forward like lightning. Suddenly, we heard a burst of bomb-like sounds coming from the west. We were invigorated by this sound, but only our hearts were shaken. Our eyes did not shift to the outside of the train window. We remained calmly seated in the car, because the most important thing for soldiers is (to observe order) and discipline. Soon, the train approached the platform. We saw compatriots welcoming us, clapping enthusiastically and shouting. Only then did I understand the sound just now came from their palms.

We got off the platform. After slightly tidying up everything, we exited the station in single file, led by the security team's music band, all the way to the Wujin County Party Department, where we stayed. That night, we were treated to a grand banquet by the county government.

Changzhou combs are renowned in Jiangsu. I still remember the spring of the eighteenth year, when my father, mother, sisters, brothers, and I were touring here. I bought two combs to take home. Now my mother and sister are still using them. Now that I have returned to the old place, seeing things reminds me of people. I can't help but think of the people at home. But I can only look at the sky and pray silently for my family's happiness. I also thought, this situation is like the Tang poem (Raising my head, I gaze at the bright moon; Lowering my head, I think of my hometown). So I took this matter—thinking of home—as poetic, as an ideal poetic sentiment. Now we should immediately abandon our pens and join the army. How can we carefully savor the sacredness of this all-encompassing poetry?

This morning (the 15th), all sectors of Changzhou held a welcome and send-off rally like Wuxi. About five or six thousand people attended. After the meeting, the attendees sent us to the station. In an instant, the platform was unbearably crowded. Those who came later had no place to stand. After three o'clock, the whistle sounded. The train moved slowly. The send-offs waved their hands frequently in farewell. Most of the female students from Changzhou Girls' Middle School were in tears, knowing that their hearts had long been wearied for the country.

On Dong Xiujia

— Zhi Jun

The newly appointed Director of the Jiangsu Construction Department, Dong Xiujia, is a senior of the students studying in the United States. His morality and writing are quite commendable. What is most commendable is that he has no hobbies in his life. Although he smokes cigarettes, he only smokes two or three a day. He never touches wine or women, and gambling is out of the question. The former Director of the Jiangsu People's Department, Hu Pu'an, worked with Dong for five or six years in the Road Administration. He once said that Mr. Dong never wasted a minute of his life. His character can be seen from this. In recent years, the film craze has risen, and almost everyone watches movies. However, Dong has lived in Shanghai for many years and still does not know where the New Guang and Guanglu theaters are. Once, there was an appointment to meet at the Odeon Theater, but he did not arrive until after 4 o'clock. People were surprised that Dong, who never broke his promises, had broken his word. After waiting another fifteen minutes, he finally arrived, covered in sweat. It turned out that he had been searching for an hour. This is also a well-known anecdote.

New Christmas Sounds

— Huang Yingdai

Time flies. The annual Christmas is here again. Westerners celebrate Christmas with friends and relatives, making it extremely lively. However, with the advancement of science today, social customs are also changing daily. And this year's Christmas has even greater changes.

Anti-Christmas Movement in Moscow Since the revolution, Russia has strongly opposed religion. All religious courses in schools are banned. This policy has not changed to this day. Every Christmas, there is also an anti-religious movement. This year, it was held in early December, two weeks before Christmas. Stores are not allowed to sell various gifts and children's toys, and all Christmas trees are cut down as much as possible in advance. At the same time, farmers are prohibited from selling Christmas trees. The intensity of Soviet Russia's opposition to religion can be seen in general.

The Great Revolution of Santa Claus Every Christmas, Western countries have the custom of giving gifts, buying candies and toys for children. However, this year, this custom has changed. Westerners believe that this method of expressing goodwill and giving gifts is too old-fashioned and should be reformed. Therefore, they all use the method of directly sending congratulations through the telephone. In addition, they use telephoto transmission to send handwritten greetings or portraits of themselves to relatives and friends. Moreover, British people who want to send their photos to relatives and friends living in Austria, Denmark, Norway, Switzerland, etc., can arrive within twenty minutes. This is extremely fast and convenient.

Airplanes Distribute Christmas Cards The British Post Office has long known in advance that there will be a large number of telephone photographs and congratulatory telegrams before Christmas, and the transportation sector will be extremely busy. Therefore, it has decided to use airplanes to deliver Christmas cards in order to be fast. It also plans to use wireless broadcasting, so that everyone can send congratulations by telegram. Australian airlines are also preparing to collect Christmas cards and New Year cards from the 18th and deliver them by plane to avoid missing the deadline.

Chicken Talks

— Master of Paper Account Copper Bottle Studio

Chicken is the only tonic product in winter. Its effectiveness is higher than that of all mutton paste, beef floss, milk, soy milk, and so on. In the past, Li Hefei ate a young chicken every day in the winter months. He was energetic and suffered no diseases or pain throughout the year. Also, the wise son of my teacher, Hu Buyi, had carbuncles on his back that were cut out with a knife. He stopped eating meat. However, the wound sank down an inch and never healed for a long time. He then killed chickens to eat with his meals, and did so every day. In less than half a month, the defect was completely filled. This is another clear proof. During the time of the late Qing Dynasty, Gao, a Taoist priest from the Baiyun Temple outside Xibianmen in the capital, was good at making diced chicken. Wanfuju on Yangmeizhu inclined street inherited his method and became famous within the forbidden palace. It was called Gao's Diced Chicken. My friend Huang Yiru stayed in the capital for a long time and once tasted it. He praised it endlessly. It is indeed a good taste.

In the past, when Tang Bin of Suiyang was an official in Wuzhong, his wife and sons wore simple clothes and ate simple food. In spring, they picked wild shepherd's purse every day and made it into soup with soybeans. Therefore, there was a saying among the people that it was like bean curd soup. One day, someone bought a chicken on the market. The public was shocked and said, "I have never eaten chicken since I came to Wu. Who bought it?" The servant kowtowed and said, "The son." The public was angry and immediately summoned the son to kneel in the courtyard and scolded him, "Do you think Suzhou chickens are cheaper than those in Henan? If you want to eat chicken, then go home. How can a scholar do anything without chewing on vegetable roots?" He also dismissed the servant and sent him away. This became a laughing stock for a time.

The ancient essayist Fang Wangxi was only four years old when his father taught him the classics every day. He once got up early, ordered the rooster to crow and challenge him to write a couplet. He immediately responded: "The dragon's breath forms clouds." Such was his intelligence.

Taihe County in Jiangxi produces brocade chickens. Their five colors are gorgeous. Former President Taft loved to raise them and fed them grains every day.

The DeMar factory uses a cold-pressing method to make chicken juice. It is sold all over Europe. As a result, it slaughters as many as 300 million chickens every year. The identification of chickens is extremely precise. The size of the chicken farms is even larger than the ancient chicken workshops.

Taiwan was originally called Chicken Cage Mountain because of its shape. Now that Taiwan has been incorporated into the Japanese territory, looking east with our heads raised, we cannot help but feel sad.

Hearing the rooster crow and dancing, this is Zu Ti's heroic spirit. When foreign insults are imminent and national disasters are at hand, our people should take Zu Ti as an example and the rooster's crow as an alarm clock. This is acceptable.

Mr. Gao Junshan Returns from Europe and America to Talk about National Disaster (7)

— Ji Ping

China is Japan's large marketplace. Therefore, if the boycott of Japanese goods can be maintained permanently, it can cause great economic losses to Japan. However, there is a danger of shaking the boycott movement. Many merchants want to sell off their inventory immediately because they have too much stock and are short of funds. There are even a few unscrupulous merchants who want to sell the registered Japanese goods unconditionally, so that they can simultaneously sell off the Japanese goods that they have privately imported later. Recently, people in society have discussed the methods for disposing of sealed Japanese goods. Among them, the most reasonable method is to put the Japanese goods aside for several months and then concentrate them for public sale. In this way, if the Sino-Japanese problem is completely resolved in the future, Japanese goods can still be imported again after economic resumption. At least Japan will have suffered losses within this period.

I believe that the Sino-Japanese problem will not have a satisfactory result. What is being contested now is only the amount of damage. As for the boycott of Japanese goods, it must be maintained permanently. From now on, our people vow to never use Japanese goods again, in order to give Japan a small economic wound. As for the Japanese goods that are currently sealed, if it is necessary to sell them urgently in order to save the money supply in the market, then a suitable location must be designated for centralized public sale in order to prevent malpractice. Now, some people are strongly opposed to centralized public sale and are making every effort to advocate free sale. All discerning people can see that this proposal is not supported by merchants who sincerely boycott Japanese goods. Only a few people have other intentions, so they made this proposal. We must all pay attention to this point at all times, so that the boycott movement, which has been so hard-won, does not fall short. This boycott relies entirely on the automatic awareness of merchants, so the results are better than the previous few times. I hope that patriotic merchants will continue to do so from beginning to end and not be manipulated by a few people. As for the general public, who have no weapons, they cannot all go to the battlefield to kill the enemy. If they want to save the country, permanently boycotting Japanese goods is a very important task. (End)

They are a perfect match. It is appropriate that both families of Xiang Wang are happy. Celebrities in Shanghai also attended the ceremony in person, making it a grand occasion for a while.

The joy of the newlyweds is immeasurable, and the merits of the hosts are immeasurable. There will be no banquet to trouble our friends to attend. We have already received much honor and favor. All customary gifts are kindly declined.) Therefore, there was no music in the hall that day, and there were no screens on the four walls. It is said that this civilianized wedding is a good example to follow today.

Rotary Club

Sharing the Same Hatred (3)

— Gu Mingdao

Chapter 5: Bloodshed on the Battlefield

Battalion Commander Ren Yuan of the artillery also said, "The Sunlight Army has reinforcements everywhere, while our army is isolated and without support. Military supplies and food are in great shortage. When we sent troops last time, we relied on the support of the Sunlight Country. Now, after two fierce battles, more than half of our supplies have been consumed. If we were to confront them head-on, I'm afraid we would be outnumbered and difficult to win. It's better to choose a strategic mountain and retreat temporarily. In the future, we can contact the troops from H province and then make plans." Hua Naiqiang nodded and said, "Very good. But I don't know the geography. Is there any strategic mountain valley nearby where we can temporarily stop?" Ren Yuan said, "Yes, yes. About sixty or seventy miles from Yejigang, there is Centipede Ridge. It is extremely secluded and dangerous. Because the entrance to the mountain is only a narrow path, and both sides are steep cliffs that are impossible to climb. It is shaped like a centipede, hence the name Centipede Ridge. It truly fits the ancient saying, 'One man guards the pass, and ten thousand men cannot pass.' If we hold on to it, even if the enemy is numerous, it will be difficult for them to penetrate. Overlooking from the ridge, everything nearby is very clear. As long as we set up cannons and bombard the enemy, it will be difficult for the enemy to cross the line of fire. Moreover, there are fields in the mountains that can be cultivated, and there are also good people living there. We don't have to worry about the lack of food." Hua Naiqiang said, "Since there is such a place, I will order the team to leave tomorrow morning." Zhong Shu said, "The most hateful thing is that the Sunlight Army relies on the power of their planes to constantly attack us. We don't have anti-aircraft guns, so we are greatly affected." Ren Yuan said, "We have flat-trajectory guns. If we turn the muzzles upward, we can also bombard low-flying planes." Hua Naiqiang said, "Then, if enemy planes come in the future, please ask Battalion Commander Ren to try it." Ren Yuan nodded and said, "Yes, yes." So everyone stayed in the camp for one night. The next morning, Hua Naiqiang got up, and Zhong Shu also came over. The two of them walked out of the camp tent and stood on the hill to breathe in the fresh air. Hua Naiqiang was about to order his subordinates to leave when he saw two black spots far away in the clouds. Before long, he heard the creaking sound of two red Sunlight Army planes heading this way. They got closer and bigger, circling in the air and gradually lowering. At this time, everyone was on alert. Hua Naiqiang and Zhong Shu stood still, unmoved. One of the planes suddenly dropped down and threw out a bomb, which landed right on the hill. Several warhorses were blown away. Hua Naiqiang remained calm, ordering his subordinates to raise their guns and wait. Then, with a bang, a cannonball flew out of the forest on the hill, hitting one of the Sunlight Army planes and falling into the deep ravine below. The other plane was so frightened that it did not dare to stay and flew back quickly. Everyone cheered. It turned out that Ren Yuan had seen the plane coming and had set up the flat-trajectory gun in the forest, with the muzzle facing upwards, waiting quietly for the plane to descend and drop its bomb. Then, he accurately fired a shot, which hit its mark. Hua Naiqiang and Zhong Shu were overjoyed and ordered their subordinates to prepare to go to Centipede Ridge, led by Ren Yuan. When they arrived in the mountains, they set up camp and cooked rice. Naiqiang, Zhong Shu, and Ren Yuan went to the entrance of the mountain to inspect the terrain. It was indeed steep and winding. Hua Naiqiang then ordered Ren Yuan to lead the artillery battalion to be stationed on the mountain, and ordered two infantry battalions to guard the entrance, forming a joint defense.

Will Bond Interest and Principal Payments Be Delayed?

People are Very Anxious, and the Market is Falling Sharply.

The Aftermarket Buying Interest Suddenly Surged, and the Market Soared.

Yesterday (December 23), the trading situation on the Shanghai Chinese Merchants Securities Exchange was as follows: The spot and futures markets were active. However, the prices of various bonds remained unstable due to market anxiety, and the market fell sharply. It was rumored that a certain party, due to financial difficulties, proposed to the central government to postpone the payment of some bond interest and principal. Upon hearing this, all parties felt extremely apprehensive. If this were confirmed, bond credibility would immediately be lost. Financial institutions holding large amounts of bonds as reserves for issuing currency would have problems with their operations. Bondholders relying on receiving interest and principal would also face immediate pressure. The severity of the situation in the bond market was unprecedented. In this situation, the government should promptly state its position to reassure the public and avoid a mutual downfall and future panic. Furthermore, the Japanese are increasingly plotting against us, increasing troops and preparing for war, and attacking Jinzhou is only a matter of time. However, our government is still undecided and has not made active preparations. All these situations have greatly increased public anxiety. The decline in bond prices is an inevitable trend. Rescue and support are now urgently needed and cannot be delayed any longer. Regarding the changes in various prices yesterday, the first session in the morning saw the sharpest decline, with vigorous selling and scarce demand. Several types of bonds almost reached the continuous decline limit compared to the previous day. The second session gradually stabilized, with some people buying at low prices, slightly raising the prices. However, market news improved in the afternoon, buying interest turned active, and prices mostly rebounded. As a result, the disarmament bonds were suspended for the next month's issue, and the current month's issue also fell sharply. Customs, Reorganization, and 1929 bonds fell by a small yuan, while 1929 Good bonds rebounded by two yuan. 2020 bonds and salt tax bonds also rebounded. The changes were quite drastic. The total spot trading volume was 38,500 yuan. The futures trading volume was 6.06 million in the morning and about 3.6 million in the afternoon, totaling 9.64 million yuan.

Downriver Rice Market Continues to Decline

Shanghai South: Yesterday, the various merchants arrived continuously, about 40 firms. There was a heavy inventory in Xuepu, the town and country stores were sluggish, and the price at the sluice market was cheap, depressing the market sentiment. The price of mid-range soft rice fell slightly. The sales of sharp-pointed rice from Luyang were flat, and the price also decreased.

New Sluice Gate: The arrival of goods from various merchants was steady but not overwhelming. In the market, the top-grade thin rice for delivery was selling well. The appetite of the merchants from the rural villages was fair, and the Maple and Lian rice sales were relatively good. The market price fell slightly. The sales of Changshu and Xixiang new rice were good, but the secondary grades were slack, and the price did not change. The sales of ocean Du sharp-pointed rice were still not good, and the price continued to fall by 5 fen. Bianyin rice still had no honor or disgrace.

Large Number of Ocean Rice Futures Contracts Traded Again

Mostly Directly Delivered to Ningbo

Yesterday, the ocean rice market situation was as follows: spot rice was fair, only 500 bags of small sizes were opened, priced at 9 yuan, 3 jiao, and 2 fen to 9 yuan, 3 jiao. They were handled by local merchants. Tianjin merchants handled 200 bags, priced at 13 yuan and 7 jiao. Vermicelli Market Hesitates

Yesterday, the vermicelli market largely remained stagnant. As delivery of the current month is approaching, most parties are settling their positions. The long positions are closing out, causing a slight decrease. However, the hedging positions are still active, causing a slight uptick. The future months were initially flat and weak, but due to the near-term conditions, they also slightly stabilized. Considering the upcoming market closure for the year, the fluctuations in the prices of various months should be small. As a result, the current month was down 2.5 li compared to the previous day, January was up 2.5 li, February was unchanged, March was up 1 fen, April was unchanged, and May was down 2.5 li.

Wheat Market Resembles Stoppage

Yesterday, the market for wheat futures was generally stagnant for all months. The current month has already passed. Due to the very few new transactions in the distant months, both buyers and sellers were mostly at a loss. There were very few transactions throughout the day. In short, the end of the year is approaching and all parties want to wind down operations, whether clients or factories, they do not want to make any changes. A definite plan will only be possible when the market reopens next year. As a result, January was down 1 fen compared to the previous day, February was down 1 fen, March and April were unchanged, and May was up 1 fen.

Local News

Various Circles Telegraph

Maintain the Credit of Public Bonds

A Matter of Social Security

Unanimous Demand for Protection

A certain Central Committee member proposed to the Fourth Plenary Session of the First Central Committee to extend the payment of principal and interest on domestic public bonds. The National Federation of Chambers of Commerce issued a declaration the day before yesterday, urging all sectors to pay attention. Yesterday, the local Silver and Money Exchange Association, the Stock Exchange Association, and the Municipal Chamber of Commerce telegraphed the Fourth Plenary Session of the First Central Committee separately, requesting attention to the credit of treasury bills and public bonds to stabilize public sentiment and maintain the financial market. Lin Kanghou of the National Federation of Chambers of Commerce also expressed his views on the matter yesterday. The various news items are summarized below.

Important Telegrams from the Financial Sector: The local Banking Association, the Money Exchange Association, and the Stock Exchange Association believe that public bonds are of great importance. They have separately telegraphed Chairman Lin of the National Government and Premier Chen of the Executive Yuan, requesting attention. The original telegram is as follows: (Submitting a statement on the importance of national debt, requesting attention.) Since the establishment of the National Government four years ago, it has issued more than 900 million yuan of domestic debt. The people have extreme trust in the government and hope that the government will have ample financial resources, political unity, engage in construction, and strive for prosperity and strength. Therefore, they spare no effort to purchase it with their hard-earned money. Under today's circumstances, the holders of various public bonds are spread throughout the country and have a great relationship with the livelihood of the people and social security. It is not just a matter for a part of the people or a part of the groups. The previous price of bonds rose and fell, but it was only a temporary phenomenon. This year, internal and external troubles have come one after another, and the price of bonds has fallen from 80% to 30-40%, and it has not stopped yet. More than half of the national property has been lost, and people's hearts are in extreme doubt. If we do not try to remedy it quickly, the national economic panic and the unemployment of the common people will create an opportunity for the communists. After the reorganization of the government, all facilities will be impossible to start. No country in the world, other than communist countries, regardless of how difficult their finances and economy are, would ever destroy the credit of their national debt on its own. Because once the credit of the debt is destroyed, construction will be impossible to raise funds, and it will inevitably be driven into communism. Therefore, once the national debt loses its value, all national property loses its value. The loss is not only to the holders of national debt, and its relationship is not only in finance and economics, but even the inherent doctrines and policies must be fundamentally overthrown. Therefore, to prevent the growth of communism, we must never arbitrarily destroy the credit of the national debt and trap the national economy in a dead end. This is the general trend of the world economy, the division between communism and non-communism. All of our people must truly recognize this in advance. What the heart feels is dangerous, how can we remain silent? We should ask your seat (the Executive Yuan) to give attention to this and to never adopt any proposals to change the national debt. Please issue a clear statement in advance to stabilize the people's hearts and restore the credit of the debt. We are anxiously awaiting your orders. Respectfully submitted to Chairman Lin of the National Government and Premier Chen of the Executive Yuan.

Telegraph from the Municipal Chamber of Commerce: The Municipal Chamber of Commerce telegraphed the plenary session of the Fourth Central Executive Committee yesterday, saying, "To the honorable members of the plenary session of the Fourth Central Committee in Nanjing: We have heard that at this meeting, someone proposed that the central government should earnestly consult with the financial community, taking into account the central government's financial difficulties and the scope of maintaining the credit of public bonds, and find ways to extend the payment of principal and interest on public bonds. If this proposal is implemented, the national commercial finance will be in danger of bankruptcy. We are deeply alarmed. We have found that our country's public bonds, such as the Yuan Eight Second Public Bonds and the Nine Six Public Bonds, have become waste paper because of the postponement of principal and interest payments. The market price of one is only about 10%. It can be asserted that the result of the proposed extension of payment of principal and interest on public bonds is that the prices of various public bonds will inevitably be reduced to the continuation of the Nine Six Public Bonds. Since the Japanese started the war and the political situation became tense, the price of public bonds has plummeted, and the huge losses suffered by the financial industry have almost broken all records. The reason why it can still make up for the security of the evening and has not broken down is that the government has announced its credit, and each period of principal and interest can still be paid to barely support the dangerous situation. Now, if there is another proposal to extend the payment of principal and interest, it is no different from fueling the flames. The result will only be that everyone will be dragged down together. Since the government has repeatedly issued domestic public bonds, the number is almost 700-800 million. Not only is it popular in the national financial industry, but also charitable organizations use it as a fund, and the people's livelihood depends on it for maintenance. If public bonds cannot maintain credit, not only will there be panic in the national finance, but the maintenance of charitable undertakings and the resources of the national livelihood will be exhausted immediately. This kind of measure is no different from drinking poison to quench thirst. It is known without deep thought that it is impossible. As for adjusting national finances, we should start by eliminating the interception of tax revenue in various places and reducing government and military expenses. If we can unify political power and strictly adhere to the budget, then there should not be no way to solve the financial problems. There are many complicated matters in this matter, and officials and the people can jointly form a financial conference to discuss the progress together. We must not seek temporary convenience and cut off the source of national livelihood to supply military and political expenses, so as to destroy the credit of the country in the future to adjust the budget and issue new bonds, and trap the national economy in an irredeemable position. We hope that you will investigate and implement it. Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce."

Declaration by Trade Associations: More than 160 trade associations in this city issued a declaration yesterday opposing the proposal by a certain Central Committee member to extend the payment of principal and interest on public bonds, saying, "The violent sun is rampant, disasters are everywhere, and internal and external troubles are invading each other. Although the people are doing their best to cry out and lament, the government has not yet shown any progress. Our merchants and people are determined to sever economic relations with Japan. Under the non-resistance policy of the authorities, it is the only weapon for the people to resist Japan. They are determined to break the boat and devote themselves to the work of resisting Japanese goods. For example, all the old Japanese goods that have been imported are sealed up. The total amount is in the tens of millions. Although the money is becoming tighter and the financial situation is becoming more dangerous, for the sake of solid resistance to Japanese goods, we would rather suffer extreme sacrifices and maintain the normal state of sealing. The depth of the suffering cannot be described. Recently, we heard that a certain Central Committee member has proposed to extend the payment of principal and interest on public bonds. We were extremely surprised and puzzled. We have found that the people have borne more than 100 million public bonds and treasury bills in the past four or five years. In peacetime, the people are eager to govern and are happy to purchase them. Although the amount of debt has plummeted due to political factors, and it can still be paid principal and interest on schedule, the people's hearts will not be confused to the extreme. Now, if we lose even this lowest level of credit for repaying principal and paying interest, at this time when the end of the year is approaching and the money is extremely tight, the severity of the disaster and the depth of the harm are really difficult to predict. Financial institutions will be the first to bear the brunt and will be unable to cope. The people across the country who rely on principal and interest income for their livelihood will inevitably declare bankruptcy and perish together. This is not waiting for the violent sun to destroy us, but we have destroyed ourselves. Our association, etc., are afraid to remain silent because of what the heart feels is dangerous. We believe that anyone who proposes to extend the repayment of principal and interest on public bonds is a culprit who destroys the national economy, and the people across the country can attack him with drums. We hereby declare this, and we hope that you will be aware of it. Shanghai Municipal Gut Industry Association, Shanghai Municipal Medicinal Materials Industry Association, Shanghai Municipal Ginseng and Bird's Nest Industry Association, Shanghai Municipal Chinese Medicine Industry Association, Shanghai Municipal Pollen Industry Association, Shanghai North-South Goods Dismantling Exchange Industry Association, Shanghai Municipal Seafood Industry Association, Shanghai Municipal Silk and Satin Industry Association, Shanghai Municipal Flying Flower Industry Association, Shanghai Silk-Cotton Textile Industry Association, Shanghai Municipal Sand and Stone Industry Association, Shanghai Municipal Color Printing Industry Association, Shanghai Municipal Cotton Cloth Industry Association, Shanghai Municipal Coal Industry Association, Shanghai Municipal Fur Industry Association, Shanghai Municipal Shoe Industry Association, Shanghai Municipal Sugar Industry Association, Shanghai Municipal Mineral Ash Factory Industry Association, etc., more than 160 associations jointly declare."

Telegrams from the Woodware Industry, etc.: The Shanghai Municipal Chinese and Western Woodware Dealers Association and the Biscuit, Candy, and Canned Food Industry Association telegraphed the Central Government yesterday, saying, "To the Nanjing Central Party Headquarters Fourth Plenary Session of the First Central Committee: Your Association is holding a meeting in the capital in the autumn of national crisis and after peaceful reunification. You are scheduled to have many plans for domestic politics, foreign affairs, and economy, so as to stabilize the country and resist foreign aggression. Unexpectedly, at the time when the violent sun has not yet returned the occupied land and is launching a large-scale attack on Jinzhou, news has come that there is a case of stopping the principal and interest of domestic public bonds and treasury bills. If it becomes a reality, the bonds will immediately become waste paper, and the credit of the Chinese National Party's government will be completely overthrown. Those who hold principal and interest to live and hold bonds to operate funds will all become dried carp. The interests are concerned, and we urgently telegraph this to you, and we are looking forward to your clear instructions so as to stabilize the people's hearts and maintain the national credit. Yang Guangxing, Chairman of the Shanghai Municipal Chinese and Western Woodware Dealers Association, Zhang Yichen, Chairman of the Biscuit, Candy, and Canned Food Industry Association."

Telegram from the Lixue United Association: The Shanghai Lixue United Association telegraphed the Central Government yesterday, saying, "To the Nanjing Chinese Kuomintang Fourth First Central Executive Supervision Committee: We are horrified to read in the newspaper that your Association has a proposal to stop paying the principal and interest on domestic public bonds and treasury bills. We have found that domestic public bonds and treasury bills have reliable funds and outstanding credit. The principal and interest are paid on schedule in accordance with the regulations. Therefore, Lixue people are vying to purchase them as a stable investment, and they receive principal and interest to support their lives. If this proposal is put forward and passed, the life and death of Lixue people will be judged immediately. We are asking the Party's government, which is calling for representing the interests of the people and liberating the suffering of the people, not to take this step of destroying the people's livelihood and destroying its credit with the people. We are telegraphing you especially to clearly announce the truth so as to stabilize the people's hearts.

Lin Kanghou's Statement: The National News Agency said that Lin Kanghou, Chairman of the National Federation of Chambers of Commerce, told the National News Agency reporter yesterday that the (Declaration on National Financial Issues) issued by the Federation yesterday was to urge the government to pay attention to debt credit and to awaken the people to pay attention to debt rights. The public bonds and treasury bills held by the financial community average only one-fifth. The majority of the bondholders are still very common merchants. Therefore, if the principal and interest on the bonds are extended for payment, the first to bear the brunt will definitely not be the financial community, but the majority of merchants. Because financial institutions, such as banks, are well prepared and will not endanger the entire business or part of the money because of the bonds that are part of their business. I am deeply afraid that the outside world will misunderstand the wording in yesterday's declaration, so I have to make this solemn statement again.

He Xiangning's Views on the Current Situation

Central Committee member He Xiangning issued her views on the current situation, saying, "It has been many years since the National Revolutionary Army set out on the Northern Expedition. The tangible warlords have been overthrown, but the intangible warlords have been replaced and produced. The old-style bureaucrats seem to have been driven out, but the new-style bureaucrats have become more intensified. Years of civil war have caused our people to suffer heavily, their essence has been lost, and their vitality has been lost. Revolution is advocated every day, but the revolution has not been successful. Unification is sung by everyone, but unification is difficult to achieve. Today, the task of saving the country and saving the people has not been completed, but instead has invited foreign insults. Everything that was not seen in the autocratic era and under the warlord politics is seen in today's revolutionary upsurge. In the past, countless fresh blood was sacrificed, and the current result is like this. In this era of the 20th century, recalling the history of more than 4,000 years, I am deeply saddened. However, the reason why this is the case is not the fault of the revolution, but the fault of a group of pseudo-revolutionaries. Sun Yat-sen, the leader of our party, separated (power) and (ability) in the principle of the people's rights of the Three Principles of the People. Power belongs to the people, and ability belongs to the government, so that all measures and actions of the government are subject to the supervision of the people, so that those in power dare not abuse their power, indulge their ambitions, and act arbitrarily, so as to harm the people. If Sun Yat-sen's claim of separating power and ability can be implemented, then the people will have the power to remove all corrupt officials. The people will have the power to stop the endless wars. The people will have the power to order the government to eliminate the excessive taxes and miscellaneous taxes that make the people unable to bear the burden. The people will have the right to criticize the bureaucrats who are despicable and love to stir up trouble with extreme freedom in public opinion. The people will have the right to remove or warn those in power who are incompetent or lazy. The people will have the right to resist the foolishness and weakness of diplomacy. The people will have the right to resist or remove the laws that are contrary to the majority of the people's wishes. In addition, the people have the absolute right to supervise all income and expenditure of national and local finances, and the government's actions and facilities that are not satisfactory to the people, so that the people's will can be expressed, and those in power dare not act arbitrarily. The people can have the right to supervise the government, and then the political situation will have the hope of improvement by gradually implementing the four powers of election (removal), (creation), and (referendum). Therefore, for me, He Xiangning, my opinion on today's domestic affairs and resisting foreign aggression is to first advocate the implementation of the right to remove officials in the principle of the people's rights set by Sun Yat-sen, so that the people can make suggestions and implement everything to the government according to their will. For example, if local officials collect excessive taxes or are corrupt and irresponsible, the people should be allowed to impeach them, reform them, or implement their removal. Secondly, in all provinces, cities, and counties across the country, where there are administrative organs, the Party and all parties, factions, non-party, and non-faction, and the gentlemen, farmers, merchants, women, soldiers, and people of each province, city, and county shall form a (People's Supervisory Committee) themselves. If the association elects people from all parties and factions who have not violated the law (the standard for violating the law should be based on the true will of the people), the government shall not remove its powers to supervise the behavior of the local governor. Supervisors shall not participate in any administrative organs or serve as officials) and judge their merits and demerits based on the true will of the people (anyone with an official position cannot participate in the Supervisory Committee). All matters that should be done and should be reformed locally shall be discussed and reformed by the local people and the local government. In recent years, there have been many natural disasters and man-made disasters in various places, and many people have died. Many brave and promising young people have also been sacrificed due to political relations. For example, Deng Yanda, who used to work hard in the revolution, was a promising and brave young man, but he was shot dead. Is it not too unloving of talents and too cruel? At this time of national crisis, people's lives should be cherished, so as to go to the national crisis together and resist Japanese imperialism. Therefore, political prisoners should be released to fight against the violent sun. After He Xiangning returned to China, in view of the national people's enthusiastic and激暴 patriotic movement, there are also some things that I cannot help but say. The Republic of China is composed of 400 million Chinese people. It is not a country of a few people in the government, but a country of 400 million people. The government is just its servant. If we do not resist foreign insults and lead to destruction, it is to destroy the country of the entire nation and make them feel pain. The people are running around and calling for the patriotic movement to love China, which has a history of thousands of years, and to love China, which was created by their ancestors through thorns and hardships. Their enthusiasm is commendable. Now, the violent sun is pressing on me step by step, and a certain country has also stationed troops in Annam, threatening to spy on my Yunnan and Guangxi. My country is really in danger. Now, students across the country have formed volunteer armies and are receiving military training. Awakened people have also spontaneously formed self-saving groups, demanding that the government declare war on Japan. If the government can carefully adopt their sincerity and give them strict military training, so that they can hold weapons to defend the country, then my great China will definitely not be repeatedly trampled on by imperialism. Recalling the vigorousness of my party and the people's spirit in the 14th year, and gaining the sympathy of the weak and small nations, so that the strong neighbors dared not humiliate me, compared with today, it is really different. Looking at all countries, when there is a national crisis, most of them implement conscription, and the whole country is armed to defend it. Why can't my country follow suit? Sun Yat-sen led the National Revolution to save China. Today, when foreign invaders are deepening, the people should rise up to overthrow Japanese imperialism. I hope that the government will have a proper study of this and give guidance, so as not to fail the people's enthusiasm, so that the people will not be disappointed. As for democratic politics, I also have some opinions to contribute. I believe that people's livelihood politics should follow the majority of the people's will. Where is the majority of the people's will? Which boundary has the most people? This should be studied and paid attention to. Only when the people truly have power can democratic politics be realized and the goal of the National Revolution can be achieved. To seek freedom and equality for China, if the people's rights are not realized, the National Revolution cannot succeed. Recently, some people have advocated that people's groups organize representative organs to discuss diplomacy together, and some have advocated that this organ should be permanently retained. There are also opinions that the location of the organ should be in Shanghai. However, although Shanghai is a convenient transportation hub, where merchants gather, and where finance is concentrated, the population only accounts for a small number of the national population. The pain of the villagers and small iron people is even deeper, and their desire for happiness is even stronger. If they truly seek the welfare of the people, it is not just the corner of Shanghai. Wouldn't that argument be wrong? Therefore, each province, city, and county across the country should also have supervisory organs, so as to collect the opinions of the majority of the people and relieve the pain of the majority. I believe that the current anti-Japanese work, the positive is to declare war, and the negative is to permanently sever economic relations with it. Internally, we should earnestly support farmers and workers and develop commerce. Then we can hope that China will be among the strong. After the East Three Provinces incident, the situation in our country has become increasingly serious. I believe that to confront Japanese imperialism, the people of our country should work together. It is also necessary to unite with the weak and small nations of the world and work together with the nations that treat me equally. Because the imperialists' invasion of the weak and small nations is a sympathetic response. Sun Yat-sen had a great vision and knew that to overthrow imperialism, it was necessary to unite with the weak and small nations and fight together. Therefore, his will said to unite with the nations of the world that treat me equally and fight together. My country is an oppressed nation, and if we cannot sympathize with other weak and small nations, then we cannot unite to overthrow imperialism. At this time when the national crisis is in full swing and foreign insults are urgent, my compatriots across the country are doing their best to raise funds to discuss ways to save the country. I would like to offer my humble opinion to the elders, brothers, and sisters across the country, hoping that they will study and discuss it. I am listed as a member of the Central Committee, and I ask myself that my virtue is thin and my ability is weak. I have nothing to offer to the party and the country, and I have nothing to benefit the people. I feel ashamed. From now on, I will resolutely resign from my post as a member of the Central Committee and concentrate on running social charitable undertakings to fulfill my responsibility as a citizen.

After the Economic Embargo

The Current Situation of Transportation and Shipping

Losses of Japanese Ships in Four Months

Totaling 97 Million

Since the Japanese troops forcibly occupied our Liaoning and Jilin provinces, Chinese people going to the Northeast to purchase goods have been interrupted, and the financial situation in Shenyang is extremely chaotic. The Japanese are bundling up cash from the Eastern Provinces and taking it away, causing a cash shortage in Liaoning and Shenyang. Since November, Liaoning and Shenyang have come to Shanghai to purchase cash and transport it to the city to circulate money. The Japanese Yokohama Specie Bank and British and American banks in this port have been buying cash on behalf of them in Shanghai and handing it over to a certain Japanese ship affiliated to the South Manchuria Railway to load it and transport it to Dalian, and then transfer it to Shenyang's national currency. In these four weeks, more than 3 million yuan have been transported away. It is currently still being transported. It is heard that the next shift (around Friday), a certain Japanese ship will leave Shanghai, and there will be another 700,000 to 800,000 yuan in cash loaded to Dalian, and then transferred to Liaoning.

American Cotton Transported to Shanghai. Since our country's economic embargo against Japan, the products of various spinning mills in Japan have not been sold to China. The American cotton purchased by various factories has greatly reduced demand due to the sharp reduction in shipments. The ginned cotton that has already been shipped out of the United States has been transshipped to Shanghai and resold to various yarn factories and weaving factories in China. In these two months, more than 420,000 pieces have arrived, and they are still being loaded. Today and tomorrow, 29,000 pieces of American cotton imported by the Shun Heng Shipping Company in this port will arrive in Shanghai. From today, within four weeks, the company will have seven more cotton transport ships, carrying about 100,000 pieces. In these four weeks, more than 100,000 pieces will be loaded and transported to Shanghai.

Japanese Ship Losses. The Japanese Shipowners Association investigated that after our country's boycott of Japanese ships, the business losses on near-sea and ocean routes amounted to 60 million Japanese yen, as reported in this newspaper. The association has now announced that the above losses are only the direct damage of reduced income from freight and passenger fares. There are also indirect and intangible losses, such as the reduced freight rates when ships are idle and dispatched, which amount to 23.35 million Japanese yen. In total, the losses suffered by Japanese ships since September 18th, both domestically and abroad, and in other ways, amount to 97 million yen. The compensation for laid-off crew members and dismissed sailors, such as severance pay, has not yet been issued, so it is not included.

Dispute Between the Rice Industry and the Anti-Japanese Association

Demanding Five Measures

At around 1:00 PM yesterday, the Shanghai Anti-Japanese Association found that the Yuanchangxin Rice Store in Wanjuma Wharf, Nanshi, was selling rice to Japanese merchants, so they detained Chen Dexiang, a partner of the store, along with more than 40 account books and took them back to the association. The store reported the matter to the Shanghai Bean and Rice Industry Association and asked for instructions. The association considered the matter important and immediately convened an emergency meeting of the industry at the association's general office in Cuixiutang, Fuyou Road, at around 3:00 PM that afternoon. Dozens of companies from the north and south cities attended the meeting. The meeting was held as usual. First, Chairman Kuai Huijun reported the purpose of the meeting. Then, Chen Bingqian, the manager of Yuanchangxin Rice Store, stated the situation at the time, saying: "At around 12:00 PM last night, two inspectors from the Shanghai Anti-Japanese Association, Song and others, came and claimed that our store had sold 30 bags of rice to Japanese merchants on October 13th of this year. Because our store has never had any dealings with Japanese merchants, we took out all the account books for them to check. As a result, these 30 bags of rice were purchased by our store from Taicheng Rice Store and sold to Jin [?] Rice Store in Guangqi Road in the city on October 13th of this year. Our store has never traded with Japanese merchants. The facts are there. Unexpectedly, the inspectors suddenly said that they had to take all the account books to the Anti-Japanese Association for review. Because the account books are related to the business of the store, we could not allow it. The inspectors left in anger. An hour later, the inspectors suddenly gathered more than a dozen companions, drove a car, and rushed to our store. Without asking why, they searched all over the store downstairs, but found no evidence. They then tried to pry open the silver box, took out more than 40 account books stored inside, and planned to take them away. Chen Dexiang, a partner of our store, stepped forward to stop them, but was brutally beaten, and even a piece of glass was broken. Soon, they twisted Chen Dexiang, along with the account books, and pushed him into the car and sped away. This kind of action by the association has a great impact on the future of the industry. Please discuss it among the industry colleagues." Representatives from companies such as Yongfeng, Hefeng, Xiefeng, Qianchang, Zhouyitai, etc. reported that similar incidents had occurred, and account books had been confiscated by the Anti-Japanese Association and have not been returned. After repeated discussions, the colleagues decided: (1) The association will first send a letter to the Anti-Japanese Association, requesting that the account books taken from Yongfeng and others and the detained partner be released immediately. (2) If the association does not resolve the matter satisfactorily, the association will not be responsible for any unfortunate incidents that occur to the industry colleagues. (3) According to this resolution, submit it to the Shanghai Municipal Government, the Municipal Social Bureau, and the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, requesting effective protection, and announce the facts to the people of the country. It was also decided to demand five measures from the Anti-Japanese Association: (1) The account books of the industry colleagues that have been taken away must be returned immediately, and Chen Dexiang, who was detained, must be released immediately. (2) Hand over the perpetrators to the authorities for severe punishment according to law. (3) Be responsible for compensating all losses suffered by the affected industry colleagues this time. (4) Guarantee that the same incident will not happen again in the future. (5) In the future, when checking account books, the association personnel must jointly check with the personnel of this association. (6) The aforementioned measures must be resolved satisfactorily within two days, otherwise, the entire industry will unanimously stop trading, and the responsibility shall be borne entirely by your association. The meeting adjourned after the decision was made.

Baoshan County Organizes Winter Defense

Sun Xiwu, the magistrate of Baoshan County, believes that the county is located on the coast and connects to Songhu, so winter defense is more important and should be organized as soon as possible to maintain security. He convened a meeting of agencies at the county government at 2:00 PM yesterday to discuss the progress. Ji Zhonghe, Zhang Yahua, Mao Shi'dan, Ding Yonghan, Gu Hongru, and others attended. Magistrate Sun chaired the meeting, and Zhang Ruyu took the minutes. The discussion resulted in: (1) The public security sub-bureaus will jointly form a guard patrol team with the militia to go out on patrol at any time and contact the local garrison. (2) Investigate the household registration of residents from other provinces in each district. (3) Rectify the long-distance telephone in each district to ensure that news is communicated in case of need. (4) A long-distance bus must be reserved at each station every night so that it can be used at any time if necessary. (5) Each village should organize a village guard team to facilitate winter defense.

The Third Anniversary of the Trademark Bureau of the Ministry of Industry

Yesterday was the third anniversary of the establishment of the Trademark Bureau. The bureau held a commemorative ceremony on that day and compiled a report on the work achievements over the years, including the following major points: (1) Regarding trademark matters, a total of 17,222 items have been registered, 1,681 items have been reviewed and announced but have not yet expired, 303 cases of resolving objections and evaluations have been completed, and other letters and approval orders amount to approximately 28,086 items, for a total of 47,292 items processed. (2) Regarding the revision of the Trademark Law, the old Trademark Law had been promulgated for many years, and there were many inconveniences in application. A draft was submitted to the Legislative Yuan for correction and promulgation in May of last year. The implementation rules were also submitted to the former Ministry of Industry and Commerce for amendment and were implemented on January 1st of this year, which is convenient for both Chinese and foreign parties. (3) Regarding the unification of trademark administrative matters, the Guangdong trademark cases were received by the bureau in June of 1929, and regulations were drafted and submitted to the ministry for promulgation and continued processing. This item has now been processed completely. 4. Regarding the promotion of domestic products, the domestic trademark approvals over the years have been compiled and printed in two issues of the "Domestic Product Trademark Gazette". The content of the gazette has been revised and updated, and those who continue to register have been added and recompiled into the "Domestic Product Trademark First Compilation" in order to arouse the attention of the domestic industrial and commercial circles and promote the development of domestic products. Director Wen of the bureau also encouraged all staff to continue their efforts during the commemorative ceremony to achieve the goal of assisting the development of industrial and commercial enterprises.

French Concession

Public Works Bureau Next Year's Budget

Balance Achieved in Regular Expenses

The "North-China Daily News" reports that the French Concession Public Works Bureau's 1932 budget has achieved a balance in regular expenses. It is estimated that within an income of 5.7 million taels, after deducting expenses, there will still be a surplus of over 5,000 taels. It is noted that the Public Works Bureau's income will decrease compared to previous years. For example, the income from the Mixed Court has no longer belonged to the Public Works Bureau since it was handed over on August 1st of this year. Similarly, the wharfage dues have also been greatly affected since the implementation of the new Chinese-foreign distribution method on May 1st. Furthermore, the Gujiazhai Radio Station's cessation of commercial broadcasting on July 15th has also reduced income. Not only will there be a decrease in income next year, but expenditures will also increase, such as the appropriate increases in salaries for Chinese and foreign staff, the interest payable on the two new public bonds this year, and the payment of garbage removal fees to the Chinese authorities. All of these will increase the burden on the municipal treasury. Therefore, to balance revenue and expenditure next year, it is necessary to slightly increase taxes to compensate. It is reported that the budget plan proposes to implement a new land price assessment in the concession inland from the second half of the year, and also increase the police tax by two percent, from thirteen to fifteen percent. Furthermore, license fees for hotels, inns, wine shops, cafes, restaurants, dance halls, etc., will increase by 25 percent. The license fees for brothels and singing girls will increase by five yuan per quarter. All retail liquor stores must obtain licenses by paying dues. License fees for public garages will also increase. In addition, there will be slight revisions to several other tax rates. Overall, in this environment, the budget can be considered sound.

Jiangsu-Zhejiang Fisheries Bureau

Haiying Patrol Ship Patrolling and Suppressing Pirates

Since his appointment, Han Yougang, Director of the Jiangsu-Zhejiang Fisheries Administration Bureau of the Ministry of Industry, has been determined to protect fisheries. He has repeatedly captured pirates during the summer and autumn seasons, which has been praised by fishermen. Currently, during the winter fishing season, the threat of pirates is even more intense, and patrols cannot be relaxed in the slightest. Therefore, even though the bureau is facing extreme financial difficulties, it is still making every effort to intensify its fishery protection work. In order to supervise and urge the various ships under his command to carry out their duties, Director Han personally went to the outer seas of Zhejiang at the end of last month to inspect them for a week, and strictly ordered the "Haiying," "Hai," "Qing'an," and "Biaohai" patrol ships to intensify patrols at all times. According to a report from the Haiying patrol ship, at 9:00 AM on the 17th of this month, when the ship was patrolling outside Jishuimen in Shipu, Zhejiang, it encountered a suspicious ship. The ship was ordered to stop for inspection, but the pirates, seeing the situation was unfavorable, resisted and fled. The Haiying patrol ship pursued them vigorously, and after a standoff of three hours, the pirates could not hold on any longer and fled ashore. Several pirates were killed and many were wounded. In addition, a captured fishing boat and a Ningbo Island sand barge were rescued, as well as twenty to thirty refugees. It is said that after this attack, the pirates in the surrounding waters have fled far away after hearing the news.

Minutes of the Standing Committee Meeting of the Jiangsu Flood Relief Association

Yesterday afternoon at 5:00 PM, the Jiangsu Flood Relief Association held its fifth standing committee meeting at the Renji Hall on Sixth Avenue. Over ten people attended, including Cheng Jingsheng, Lu Shaoquan, Huang Hanzhi, Wang Yiting, Weng Yinchu, and Wen Lanting. Sun Yinting attended as an observer. Wang Yiting chaired the meeting, and Xiao Zhantong recorded the minutes. Items reported: (1) The association received 427 documents from various counties regarding flood relief, from November 16 to December 22. (2) The association issued 375 documents for daily operations. (3) The Provincial Relief Committee decided to handle winter relief funds for Gaoyou, Xinghua, Jiangdu, Dongtai, Baoying, Yancheng, Funing, Gaochun, Taixian, Jiangning, Huai'an, Siyang, Huaiyin, Lianshui, Yixing, Liyang, Jiangpu, Yizheng, Liuhe, Tongshan, Zhenjiang, Xiaoxian, Suqian, Jiangyin, Jingjiang, Changshu, Fengxian, Shuyang, Taicang, Jintan, Kunshan, Yangzhong, Peixian, Dangshan, Suining, Pixian, Jurong, Donghai, Taixing, Lishui, Danyang, Wujiang, Rugao, Chongming, Nantong, Qidong, Ganyu, Baoshan, Haimen, and Guanyun, Jiading and other 51 counties. The Provincial Relief Committee and the Association will each be responsible for half. The Association has also appointed personnel to investigate and distribute funds in these counties. The names of the chief and deputy directors of the investigation and distribution in each county, as well as the original plan for the allocation of relief funds and the additional amount allocated by the Association, are listed in detail in a separate table for public viewing. (4) Funds for Rugao, Chongming, Nantong, Qidong, Ganyu, Baoshan, Haimen, Guanyun, and Jiading have been requested from the Provincial Relief Committee to be directly allocated to the county governments or county sub-committees to carry out industrial relief projects. (5) Winter relief situation in various counties. (6) The disaster situation in Wujin is very serious. Standing Committee Member Wen Lanting requested that relief be provided, and 3,000 yuan has been approved and entrusted to Mr. Feng Xiaoqing to oversee the implementation. (7) The amount of relief funds and goods received by the Association. (8) The amount of relief funds and goods disbursed by the Association. (9) The amount of relief goods distributed by the Association. Matters for discussion: (1) Standing Committee Member Huang Hanzhi and Standing Committee Member Yi Qing proposed that a plan for opening up the Maoyou River and repairing the breached embankments, drafted by layman Gao Henian of Liuzhuang, be handled and requested a resolution. (Resolution) Opening up the Maoyou River requires a large amount of funds. The Association can publicize this and request the National Government's Flood Relief Committee to include it in its work scope and implement the opening. As for the embankment of the Dafeng Company, which was previously resolved, 5,000 to 6,000 yuan in industrial relief funds should be allocated in the spring to repair it. (2) Standing Committee Member Wang Yiting, Standing Committee Member Huang Hanzhi, and Standing Committee Member Yi Qing proposed that this winter relief effort is being jointly undertaken by the Provincial Relief Committee and the Association, with 600,000 yuan being allocated, each responsible for half. The current funds of the Association are insufficient, and requests for additional funds from various counties are pouring in. It is impossible to cope without raising a large amount of relief funds. How should we raise funds? Please make a resolution. (Resolution) The funds needed for winter relief should be temporarily borrowed from banks. At the same time, fundraising efforts should be intensified. The meeting adjourned.

Cultural Organizations Form a Joint Association

Discussion Meeting at the World and China Society

Since the September 18th Incident, various organizations have been forming anti-Japanese associations, united in their opposition to foreign aggression. Shanghai is the cultural center of the country, and cultural organizations are the vanguard of leading the people. However, a joint association of cultural organizations is still lacking. In view of this, the World and China Society initiated the association. Members already include the Liuhuo Monthly Society, the Literature and Art News Society, the Reading Magazine Society, the People's Voice Weekly, and the China News Agency, all organized by famous scholars and university professors in Shanghai. A discussion meeting was held at the World and China Society on the afternoon of the day before yesterday at 7:00 PM. The main purpose is to oppose imperialist military aggression against foreign countries and call on all countries regarding the recent Japanese attack on Jinzhou. Domestically, they request absolute freedom of speech, publication, and association. The date of the general meeting is set for the 25th of this month.

Mingde Principal's Embezzlement of Donation Case

Thoroughly Investigated by the Municipal Party Headquarters

Embezzled Over 2,100 Yuan

According to the "Guomin She", the students of the Sixth District Party Headquarters and Mingde Middle School have successively reported that Wu Mengyan, the principal of Mingde School, embezzled donations from all circles to General Ma Zhanshan. The details of the case, as reported in various newspapers previously, were not very clear. It has now been thoroughly investigated by Zhao Erchang, a member of the Civil Training Section of the Municipal Party Headquarters. The results of the audit show that the principal embezzled a total of 2,117.10 yuan from the donations, which has been reported to the Municipal Executive Committee for review. The details are as follows: (Sole Proprietorship) All procedures for the fundraising were handled by the principal. Donation tubes were added at any time. The student association's seal was kept by the principal, and the filled tubes were also kept by the principal. The entire arrangement made it easy to manipulate things. (Adding Printed Cards) The school's broken tubes were after 10:00 PM on November 23, but on November 25, Xu Qiong Zhang, the female teacher, added various cards in the Four Horses Road in the Minyi printing house, fifty sheets of paper worth five yuan, one thousand sheets of paper for one yuan, one thousand sheets of paper for four cents, two thousand sheets of paper for two cents each. What is the use of these cards? It is self-evident. Moreover, the school principal did not mention additional printing in previous investigations. It was not until the officials of the Municipal Party Committee held the card paper voucher to the school that they began to tell the truth. This is a planned fraud, which is clearly obvious. (Embezzlement is Real) According to the school, the total number of cards printed, minus the cards used, is equal to the remaining cards. The remaining cards verify the cards used, converted into donations, should be 3,999.50 yuan, but the principal announced that it was only 1,782.40 yuan. In comparison, the difference is 2,117.10 yuan. The number of 2,117.10 yuan is the amount embezzled by the principal.

Woman's Appeal Deemed Not Guilty

Police Lawyer Dissatisfied

Remanded During Appeal Period

Zhu Zhang, a local woman and owner of the Nanyang Department Store at No. 100 Yangzhou Road, had a minor dispute with her husband, Zhu Shisheng, over funeral arrangements for a daughter around 6:00 PM on June 24th of this year. The Western Detective of the French General Police Station stated that there have been cases of counterfeit money being used in the concession recently. Therefore, he specially instructed all Chinese and foreign detectives to pay close attention to the investigation and arrest of the suspects. Jin Jiulin, a special detective inspector of the French Police Station, and detectives Li Yaolong, Qian Yumin, and Zhang Ziying, Mao Jingen, etc., discovered that a private counterfeit money printing operation was set up at No. 78 Jianye Lane, Fuli Road. At 10:00 AM yesterday, they led detectives such as Qin Youyu and Zhou Buguang to rush to the scene, guarded the front and back doors, and broke into the house.
